Soviet Union's "Constitution Day"

75,000 Athletes Celebrate in Moscow

(Moscow) The Soviet Union has designated today as Constitution Day. 75,000 athletes held a four-hour demonstration in Red Square, holding various flags with slogans such as "Long Live Stalin" and "Long Live the Constitution." Stalin inspected the parade from the Lenin Mausoleum. (6th National Telegram)

(Moscow) The Soviet Union celebrated Constitution Day nationwide, with major cities holding grand sports parades. The Moscow sports parade was held in Red Square, attended by Stalin, Molotov, Kalinin, and other party and government leaders, who were greeted with enthusiastic cheers from tens of thousands of people. Kharchenko, Chairman of the Federal Sports Committee, and Kosarev, Secretary of the Communist Youth League, delivered speeches successively. The ranks of various Moscow sports associations marched past the Lenin Mausoleum and were reviewed by party and government leaders. The changes in their formations were extremely impressive. They were responsible for various activities in the sports field. Athletes performed swimming, cycling, tennis, and other skills on stage. Team ball teams also performed ball skills during the march, and there were other sports and boxing parade performances. Seven thousand members of the Dynamo Sports Association held up eleven women, representing the eleven republics in the draft constitution. This review began at 1 p.m. and ended at 4 p.m. The second part of the celebration was a mass exercise by 3,000 Moscow athletes, followed by exercises by 500 Ukrainian athletes and Ukrainian folk dances. After some performances, members of the Spartak Sports Association gathered in Red Square to form a football field. After a running race, a football match followed, and finally a sports parade. The participants in the parade shouted and cheered in unison, congratulating Stalin and the members of the Political Bureau of the Central Committee of the Communist Party. The parade ended at 8 p.m. (7th TASS Dispatch)

Germany Assures Britain and France: No Desire to Disrupt European Situation

Eden Acknowledges the Danzig Issue Remains Serious - Over 100 Opposition Party Members Arrested in Danzig

(London) During last night's Cabinet meeting, Foreign Secretary Eden strongly stated that the current situation in Danzig contains serious possibilities. The Cabinet will continue to consider this matter at its meeting on Wednesday. (6th Reuters)

(Berlin) The British and French ambassadors visited the German Foreign Ministry this evening to meet with Foreign Minister Neurath. As Mr. Neurath was away on official business, they were received by another official. This official assured them that Germany has no intention of taking any steps that would disrupt the current international situation. It is reported that the two ambassadors also inquired about Germany's attitude toward the speech made by Danzig Senate President Greiser at the League of Nations Administrative Council on July 4. The spokesperson replied that the German government fully supports this speech. (6th Reuters Dispatch)

Today, he spent the entire day consulting with officials of the National Socialist Party. The subject of their discussion has not been announced. Danzig: Senate President Greiser returned here today, but local residents did not give him a "warm welcome." Only a small number of National Socialists and stormtroopers greeted him at the station. This is because Greiser requested that special preparations for the welcome be canceled. It is widely believed that both Berlin and Danzig do not want to stir up trouble, hence Greiser's request. Germans Advocate for a Plebiscite on Danzig

Resolving the Future Sovereignty Issue

(Berlin) Danzig Free City Senate President Greiser visited here a few days ago and held talks with National Socialist Party officials until midnight before hurrying back to the city. Diplomatic circles here have recently expressed their views on the situation in the city, stating that the current system in the city may be changed through a plebiscite. Regarding this matter, Danzig National Socialist Party branch leader Forster made a suggestion when he met with Führer Hitler and Aviation Minister Göring. German sources also said that if the city holds a plebiscite, Germany has a good chance of winning, just like the Saar region plebiscite in January of last year. (7th Havas)

Warsaw: Danzig Free City Senate President Greiser and reporters from the city's newspapers departed from Geneva together by plane. En route, he made a statement to a reporter from the National Socialist Party's newspaper Vorwärts, stating that "The Free City of Danzig has sovereignty, but the High Commissioner of the League of Nations is now interfering in its internal affairs. This situation cannot be allowed to continue, and it must be permanently eliminated." Political figures are paying close attention to Greiser's remarks. (6th Havas Dispatch)

(London) Conservative MP Sandys, known for his pro-German stance, advocated in the House of Commons today that a plebiscite be held in the Free City of Danzig to decide the future of the Free City. Foreign Secretary Eden replied that "The Danzig issue should be handled in accordance with the provisions of the Treaty of Versailles. The countries most closely related to this issue are Germany and Poland. This is something that Mr. Sandys should pay attention to." Another MP asked the Foreign Secretary whether the British government intends to negotiate with the German government regarding Germany's current construction of defensive fortifications in the Rhineland. The Foreign Secretary replied that "The government is still willing to conduct general negotiations with the countries concerned and Germany in order to resolve various issues. Therefore, the issue of the Rhineland defensive fortifications should not be raised unilaterally by Britain to Germany." (6th Havas Dispatch)

(London) The Cabinet held a meeting this afternoon in the Cabinet Room of the House of Commons. First, they listened to Foreign Secretary Eden's report on the proceedings of the League of Nations General Assembly and the Administrative Council meeting, which was duly noted. Next, they studied the issue of the city of Danzig, and finally, they discussed the future meetings of the signatory countries of the Locarno Pact. According to sources in political circles, the most important issue discussed at today's Cabinet meeting was the issue of the city of Danzig. As a result of their deliberations, the Cabinet members unanimously agreed that the President of the Senate of the Free City of Danzig, Greiser, had made arrogant statements at the Administrative Council of the League of Nations, saying that he was speaking on behalf of the entire German nation. The implication of these words was that German Führer Hitler not only considered himself a representative of Germany, but that all nations that speak the German language, including the city of Danzig, the Memel Autonomous Region, and the residents of Austria, as well as the minority ethnic groups within the territory of Czechoslovakia, were all represented by him. It is reported that because the Polish government recently promised to adopt a firm attitude to deal with Germany, the Cabinet decided to temporarily leave the Danzig issue to Poland to handle. If Poland fails to fulfill its promise, the British government will submit the issue to the League of Nations for handling again. But in any case, when the Locarno Conference is held in the future, the Danzig issue will definitely be brought up for discussion. In addition, regarding the British list of questions, the German reply will definitely be ambiguous and difficult to understand. In order to fully understand Germany's views, the British government will request that the League of Nations be invited to attend the second stage of the Locarno Conference in order to provide oral explanations on the points in Germany's future reply that are still unclear, and that this is a necessary condition for Germany's participation in the Locarno Conference. The British Cabinet now hopes that the Locarno Conference will not only discuss the issue of re-establishing the original spirit of the Locarno Pact, but also study the issue of resolving the general situation in Europe. Before the European situation is resolved, the temporary measures that Britain had previously promised to aid France and Belgium will naturally remain in effect. However, the permanent measures to protect the borders of the two countries contained in the annex to the previous letter to the two countries will not be considered at this time. (6th Havas Dispatch)

German-Austrian Negotiations Break Down: Hitler Rejects Four Conditions

(Vienna) According to official sources today, the negotiations between Germany and Austria for reconciliation have broken down, and Austrian Chancellor Schuschnigg believes that there is currently no possibility of a solution. It is said that Schuschnigg, through the German Ambassador Papen, conveyed four conditions to German Führer Hitler: 1. Germany fully recognizes the independence of Austria; 2. Germany allows Austria not to interfere in its internal affairs; 3. Germany recognizes that Austria has full autonomy in all matters concerning Austria, such as the restoration of the monarchy, etc.; 4. Hitler abandons the Austrian National Socialist Party. After these conditions were put forward, the negotiations failed, and Schuschnigg has decided to base his political policy on the restoration of the Habsburg dynasty in order to avoid the National Socialist Party controlling Austria. (6th National Telegram)

(Vienna) The reconciliation negotiations between Austrian Chancellor Dr. Schuschnigg and German Ambassador to Austria Papen, which took place in the middle of last week, have failed, so there is no hope of easing the current serious situation. It is reported that the failure of the negotiations was due to Germany's demand to allow the National Socialist Party in Austria to freely express its opinions and carry out "cultural work," and to pay attention to anti-Jewish actions. Germany also refused to agree to the restoration of the Habsburg dynasty. The main conditions put forward by Austria were that Germany declare respect for the current borders and allow non-interference in Austria. If so, then Stalin would grant amnesty to the Austrian National Socialist Party criminals. (6th Reuters Dispatch)

American Song and Dance Star Donates Entire Fortune to Charity

Terrytown, New York: Miss Jenness, a song and dance star who is very famous in the song and dance world, announced today that she intends to sell all her possessions and use the proceeds to start a charity. She did this because she was touched by the power of God. Dozens of people hoping to share in the blessings of this inspiration have surrounded the lady seeking help. (7th Reuters Dispatch)

Montreux Conference Discusses British Amendment

Soviet Union Temporarily Takes a Reserved Attitude - Italy Declares It Will Still Not Participate

Montreux: The Montreux Conference recently held a plenary session and decided to use the plan proposed by the British representative this morning as the basis for discussion. This plan is an amendment to the new convention draft proposed by Turkey. The Soviet Union is not very welcome to this amendment, but the Turkish representative has reached a compromise with the British representative in Geneva, so it is accepted. Here are the main points:

The Turkish draft proposed that for any non-Black Sea littoral country, the number of warships allowed to pass through the straits during peacetime be limited to one cruiser and two destroyers, and that the total tonnage not exceed 14,000 tons. It is now proposed to change this to 15,000 tons. The original draft proposed that the total tonnage of warships allowed to stay in the Black Sea from non-Black Sea littoral countries not exceed 28,000 tons, which is now proposed to be changed to 30,000 tons, and may be increased to 45,000 tons in special circumstances.

In the event of a threat of war, Turkey may only close the straits with the approval of a two-thirds majority of the League of Nations General Assembly.

The original draft proposed that the tonnage and number of warships from various countries passing through the straits during wartime should be the same as during peacetime. It is now proposed that during wartime, warships from various belligerent countries may freely pass through the straits to pursue enemy warships without any restrictions.

The Turkish draft did not mention the existing Straits Commission. It is now proposed that the commission should continue to exist, but its organizational law should be formulated separately, and its future functions should focus on preparing statistics and providing information.

Any warship from another country with a mission of courtesy visits or invitations may be invited by Turkey to pass through the straits without restriction.

Once the countries concerned have signed, the new convention will immediately take effect. The signatory countries may conclude a separate protocol with Turkey, allowing the country to install defensive fortifications in the straits area.

The Turkish draft originally proposed that the new convention be valid for 15 years, which is now proposed to be changed to 50 years, with a revision allowed every five years.

In addition, at today's meeting, the Turkish delegation also agreed to reduce the health tax levied on commercial ships from various countries passing through the straits by 60%. (6th Havas Dispatch)

Montreux: The Dardanelles Straits Conference reconvened here today to consider the draft of the new convention proposed by Turkey. Britain proposed an amendment to resolve the issue of the straits' fortifications and set a term of 50 years. This amendment is contained in a memorandum that stipulates the tonnage of warships allowed to pass through the straits. However, there is another clause that stipulates that in the event of a war in which Turkey maintains neutrality, the belligerent countries have the right to send an unlimited number of troops into the Black Sea. In addition, it is also stipulated that if Turkey believes that its country is threatened by war, it has full discretion over the passage of foreign ships through the straits, and it is also stipulated that a straits commission be established and bear special and limited responsibilities. Soviet Foreign Commissar Litvinov stated that he intends to reserve his attitude towards the British amendment until he receives instructions from his government. However, the Soviet authorities will definitely not be as satisfied with the British proposal as they were with the original Turkish plan. The British proposal would prevent the 23,000-ton Soviet battleship Paris Commune, which is docked in the port of Sevastopol, from sailing out, and would also prevent the Soviet Union from maintaining a fleet of warships in the Black Sea to deal with war. (6th Reuters Dispatch)

(Rome) Political circles here are now warning the great powers not to assume that Italy will accept any agreement created in Montreux. If the Black Sea becomes a Soviet lake with a fleet of ships that can freely enter the Mediterranean, the balance of power in Italy's inland sea will change. Italy may deem it necessary to expand its navy. (6th Reuters Dispatch)

(Rome) Italy officially announced today that it has no intention of participating in the Montreux Conference. All European observers were shocked by this news. Since European countries have already reached a compromise with Italy on the Abyssinian issue, Italy could have actively participated in the conference. This announcement was truly unexpected. (6th National Telegram)

Japanese Consulate General in Chengdu Reopens

(Tokyo) The Japanese Consulate General in Chengdu, Sichuan Province, which has been closed since the Manchurian Incident, has recently decided to reopen. Iwai Eiichi, the current secretary of the Japanese Embassy in Shanghai, has been dispatched to Sichuan to act as Consul General. Iwai is now in Tokyo preparing to depart. (7th Allied Dispatch)

International Conference to Be Held in Java Next Spring

(London) During today's meeting of the House of Commons, Labor MP Tunnahill raised a question to the government, saying that the League of Nations Administrative Council has consulted with the governments of the Near East, Middle East, and Far East on the problem of trafficking in women and children in the Orient. Can the results be heard? Tokyo Mutiny Case Concludes: Verdict in the February 26 Incident: 17 Key Culprits Sentenced to Death

13 Junior Military Officers and 4 Civilians

Other Soldiers Who Acted Under Duress Were All Found Not Guilty

(Tokyo) The army's young officers, who aimed to "Showa Restoration" and murdered several key ministers, shook the world. This so-called February 26 Incident, after careful trial by the army's military court, and until 2 a.m. on the 7th, the army released the verdict document. The content is as follows:

The military court trial, regarding the February 26 Incident, involved one general, twenty former generals (of which two committed suicide immediately after the incident), three training officers, three non-commissioned officers, eighty-nine former non-commissioned officers and non-commissioned officers, three hundred and fifty-eight soldiers, and ten civilians. Among them, those accused by the authorities were one general, eighteen former generals, two non-commissioned officers, seventy-three former non-commissioned officers and non-commissioned officers, nineteen soldiers, and ten civilians. The verdict was announced on July 5 as follows: Former Army Infantry Captain Kiyosada Banda, Teruzo Ando, Lieutenant Anahide Kurihara, Katsuo Tsuishima, Tsuguo Takeshima, Takiaki Nakahashi, Seichu Moiki, Tadashi Sakai, Masaru Tanaka, Second Lieutenant Kanji Nakajima, Yu Yasuda, Hachiro Hayashi, Taro Takahashi, and civilians Takaji Muranaka, Asakazu Isobe, Zensuke Shibukawa, and Genichi Mizukami, the seventeen people recorded above, were all sentenced to death.

This morning at 2 a.m., the Army Ministry announced the main text of the February 26 Incident verdict and, at the same time, released its written reasons. The content details the causes, motives, plans, and preparations, and an overview of the actions. The final conclusion states that among the defendants, the generals, former generals, and important civilians, their feelings of deep concern for the country during this extraordinary situation, and the various matters in which some of the defendants decided to advance or retreat, are not without points that can be understood. However, their actions violated the imperial rescript, disregarded the national constitution and laws, disrupted the original meaning of the national army, and commanded the imperial army arbitrarily, stemming from rebellious behavior. Their crimes can be said to be serious. One part of the non-commissioned officers and soldiers who are guilty formed parties, armed themselves, and automatically participated in the rebellion. However, the other soldiers, etc., had no intention of participating, but due to obeying the orders of their superiors, and as comrades and other troops continued to move out, under these circumstances, they could not refuse to act. Moreover, after the incident occurred, they only acted according to orders, and now there is a clear indication of repentance. For these soldiers, the execution of their sentences is suspended. All the other soldiers are found not guilty. (7th Allied News Agency Dispatch)

(Tokyo) Nomura Saburo, a former officer candidate who was a defendant in the May 15 Incident, has been recuperating at his family home in Hirosaki City since being released from prison. Recently, through the mediation of a senior colleague, he joined the "Manchukuo" Army. He left Hirosaki for Manchuria on the 6th. (7th Allied Dispatch)

(Berlin) Dai Jitao, President of the Examination Yuan of China, arrived in Germany as the government representative of the 11th Olympic Games. Chinese Ambassador Cheng Tianfang, overseas Chinese, the Director of the Far East Department of the German Ministry of Foreign Affairs, and an assistant to the Protocol Department were all at the station to greet him. Mr. Dai expressed his gratitude to those who welcomed him. (Havas dispatch, 7th)

(Berlin) Dai Jitao, President of the Examination Yuan of China and the government representative for the Olympic Games, arrived here this morning from the capital of Sweden. Afterwards, he gave a speech to our reporter, explaining the purpose of his trip. He said, "The reason for coming to Germany is to personally study education issues. I am very interested in the political evolution of Germany, especially the issues of national education, physical education, and military training. I believe that I will benefit greatly from meeting with Defense Minister General von Blomberg in the future regarding this matter." Mr. Dai is a famous politician. He then expressed his views on Sino-German relations, saying, "I hope that the relationship between China and Germany will become increasingly close. As for Sino-German trade, its total volume has already exceeded that of Sino-British trade by 3%. The quantity of German machinery exported to China is also higher than that of Britain and the United States. In addition, Germany has provided capital and materials for the Zhe-Yi Railway (that is, the railway from Hangzhou through Nanchang and Pingxiang, connecting with the Yuehan Railway). This railway has great value in terms of economy, politics, and military strategy. Regarding domestic affairs, I firmly believe that our great leader, General Chiang Kai-shek, will be able to effectively unify China. As for Sino-Japanese relations, Japan is China's neighbor, and we should achieve genuine peace with them. However, the key to making this a reality lies with Japan." (Havas dispatch, 7th)

France is currently preoccupied with European affairs and has no time to focus on the Far East. However, for the sake of its interests in China, its political attitude remains unchanged. US Naval Espionage Case

Thompson Sentenced to Fifteen Years

Los Angeles A retired US Navy corporal named Thompson was sentenced to fifteen years imprisonment today for espionage. Several of his accomplices are important figures among Japanese residents in Los Angeles, but officials refused to release their names. (National News Agency dispatch, 6th)

Los Angeles A retired US Navy lower-ranking officer, Thompson, was accused of violating espionage laws by secretly reporting information about national defense to Japan. After it was proven that the crime was indeed committed, he was sentenced to fifteen years of exile today. Since Thompson was young, he was spared the maximum punishment of twenty years. Thompson confessed to providing information about major US fleet maneuvers to Japan and receiving a reward of 700 yuan per year. (Reuters dispatch, 7th)

Many Italian Soldiers in Addis Ababa Slit Their Throats in One Night

Ethiopians Intensify Resistance as Rainy Season Arrives

(Cairo) Mr. Holmes, a former Reuters correspondent with the Italian army in the north, arrived here today from East Africa. He said that the Italian army will face a severe test when the rainy season begins in Ethiopia. Although the Italian army claims that the banditry situation in Ethiopia is not serious, it will still take many years to quell it. During the recent St. Michael's Festival, Ethiopians all swore to drive the Italian army out of Ethiopia. However, they plan to take action only after heavy rains frequently fall and Italian aircraft cannot operate. The Italians believe that the Ethiopians are more concerned with looting than resisting the Italian army. However, in the past two months, armed and well-equipped bandits have fiercely resisted the Italian army. One night, many Italian soldiers in Addis Ababa had their throats slit. The Italian authorities arrested dozens of suspects, including some Europeans. Although many were later released, the remaining ones were either forced to build roads or were beaten in prison. Italian troops are stationed in large cities because of difficult transportation with the interior and do not dare to venture far. Hundreds of Italian troops in Asba Safare are surrounded by thousands of armed Ethiopians. The Italian authorities say they currently have no way to rescue them. (Reuters dispatch, 6th)

Soviet Military Industry Develops Rapidly; Japan Seeks Countermeasures

Plans to Actively Develop Heavy Industry in Manchuria

(Tokyo) Recently, the Soviet Union's military industry has developed greatly due to the successful completion of its two Five-Year Plans. It has built an industrial zone in the Far East, so it will no longer be necessary to transport military supplies from Europe to the Far East. The independence of military supplies in the Far East has already been established, which is particularly noteworthy. As for the Soviet Union's production capacity, according to the production plan for this year published by the Soviet Union, it is 14.5 million tons of pig iron, 16 million tons of steel, 135 million tons of coal, 30 million tons of kerosene, 4,000 aircraft, and 400 tanks. Furthermore, regarding the construction of industrial zones, after the completion of the Donbas industrial zone, the construction of Kuznetsk (a large-scale heavy industrial zone), Krivoy Rog (centered on the iron industry), Angara (a heavy industry based on hydroelectric power, accounting for 46% of the Soviet Union's total power generation), Bereznikovsky, and Sougaravan will all be actively carried out. As for quasi-military industries, various manufacturing plants for aircraft, automobiles, and weapons are being established in Khabarovsk, Irkutsk, Yuzhno-Sakhalinsk, and other places. The Japanese Army, in view of the rapid progress of the Soviet Union's heavy industrial zones, plans to develop various resources in Manchuria and promote the development of heavy industry in conjunction with the new national defense preparation plan. Therefore, it will change the previous policy of developing Manchurian industries to a heavy industry-first principle. Based on the development of industry, urban planning will be carried out. In the future, heavy industrial zones will be built in "Manchukuo." If this plan materializes, the previously restricted development of iron and coal in Manchuria, as well as the aluminum industry, will flourish. Full efforts will also be devoted to coal liquefaction, etc. (Reuters dispatch, 7th)

Singapore Learns Political and Defense Tactics

Testing the Defense Forces' Ability to Resist Attacks

(Singapore) A secret exercise was held here last night. The attacking forces launched a night attack on the southeastern coast of Singapore, fiercely attacking various key points. The defending reinforcements immediately rushed to the scene to fight back, and finally drove back the enemy forces with rifles, machine guns, and artillery. This exercise was intended to test the ability of Singapore's defense forces to respond to sudden attacks. (National News Agency dispatch, 7th)

Anglo-Egyptian Negotiations Proceed Smoothly

Cairo The Anglo-Egyptian treaty negotiations are now in their final stages. It is said that both sides are very satisfied. A legal expert from the British Foreign Office has arrived here to assist in drafting the treaty. It is expected that the representatives will travel to London before the end of the summer to sign the treaty. The authorities have not disclosed the contents of the treaty, but the public believes that the following points are reliable:

The treaty will be of a nature of alliance and friendship.

British troops will withdraw from Cairo and be stationed in Ismailia.

Egypt will ultimately be responsible for the defense of the country and the Suez Canal. However, the number of British troops stationed in Egypt will be reduced only after the Egyptian army has been sufficiently strengthened.

Egypt will be responsible for building a network of military roads so that troops can be quickly deployed to the east and west.

The British air force stationed in Egypt will be greatly increased. Large new airfields will be built in Abu Qir and Ismailia.

An important British naval base will be established in Alexandria. Britain plans to pay rent, or perhaps even establish an army base.

In the past, Anglo-Egyptian negotiations have often failed due to the Sudan issue. Although this issue has not yet been resolved, it is now believed that a solution can be found soon. As for the issue of the "conditions of surrender" in the past, it is expected to be put aside for the time being. The Arabic newspapers all carry the above outline and welcome it. (Reuters dispatch, 7th)

Situation in Jerusalem Remains Serious

Strikes and Lockouts Intensify; Bloodshed Continues

Jerusalem Lieutenant Colonel Har-El and a British soldier were injured today while providing escort work near Tulkarem, forty miles north of here, when they were ambushed by mountain Arabs. A bomb exploded at a police station near Jaffa, injuring two civilians. No one in the station was injured. Three Christian Arabs were killed in Jaffa today. It is now believed that this was the result of a family dispute. The strike plan is now intensifying, so the seriousness of the situation cannot be considered to have eased. Many stores in Jaffa that had reopened, and several stores in Jerusalem that had opened, have now closed again due to pressure. Street vendors are also unable to do business safely. In addition to being beaten, the fruits they sell are also doused with gasoline. The resurgence of the riots is now believed to be due to telegrams of encouragement received by the Arab delegation in London. At the same time, the British authorities are now implementing more stringent plans to stop the smuggling of weapons. Heavy guards are stationed at the border and other places. A British destroyer patrols the coast at night, stopping and searching any suspicious ships. (Reuters dispatch, 7th)

Legislative Yuan Reviews Income Tax Bill

Referred Back to Two Committees for Review The Bill Has Been Amended and Passed The Yuan Session Will Reconvene on the 9th to Review

(Nanjing) After passing routine motions at the meeting on the 7th, the Legislative Yuan reviewed the report of the Finance Committee on the examination of the Provisional Income Tax Regulations Bill. The committees had heated debates on the tax rates and collection methods of the regulations. After the chairman's vote, the bill was referred back to the Finance Committee to be jointly reviewed by the Economic Committee and five committee members: Luo Ding, Yang Gongda, Cheng Zhonghang, Lin Bin, and Lu Zhiyi. A special Yuan session was scheduled to reconvene at 3:00 PM on the 9th for review. At the beginning of the review of the bill, Chen Changheng reported on the review process, stating that China's central tax system has always emphasized indirect taxes, and the people feel that the burden is uneven. Direct taxes should be gradually reformed. The decision of the Central Political Committee to establish the principle of income tax has been thoroughly researched. However, because the income tax is similar in nature to the income donation collected by the central government, it has not been implemented for fear of double taxation. Now, because the cultural education expenses that rely on income donation revenue have been transferred to the national treasury for expenditure in the national budget for the 25th year, the central government has agreed to suspend the income donation. Therefore, it has been decided to levy income tax. The draft income tax regulations bill originally proposed by the Ministry of Finance only collected taxes on two types of income: business profit income and salary and remuneration income, estimated at 5 million yuan. The Finance Special Committee of the Central Political Committee expanded its scope of collection, adding a type of income: securities deposit income. Based on this type of tax revenue alone, it should be more than 15 million yuan. The total tax revenue from the three types is estimated to be at least 25 million to 30 million yuan per year. As for agricultural income and land and property income, due to the bankruptcy of the rural economy and the excessive burden on farmers, and because housing donations are already being collected, and land value tax and value-added tax will be levied in the future, they are not included in order to avoid increasing the burden on farmers. Subsequently, the three types of tax rates, tax-free scope, and collection methods in the bill were explained one by one. Liu Zhendong then provided a supplementary report, stating that this bill has been repeatedly studied by the Ministry of Finance, the Finance Special Committee of the Central Political Committee, and experts and scholars, and the following eight principles have been determined: The first type of business profit income is different from other countries in that it uses total income as the standard for taxation. Because China's commercial accounting system has not yet been established, it cannot use net income as the basis for taxation. The second type of salary and remuneration income is heavier than in other countries, but lighter than the current income tax rate. The third type of securities deposit income is to prevent capital flight and deposit accounts from being broken down into smaller amounts, so a progressive system is not adopted, but a common tax rate is set. Finally, it was stated that the tax proposed is new, so the scope is small and the tax rate is low. Cheng Zhonghang said that the tax rate in the Finance Committee's review amendment seems heavier than the one stipulated in the original draft sent by the Ministry of Finance. Is this a special favor from the Ministry of Finance, or is it increasing the burden on the people? The Finance Committee should be asked to explain further. Liu replied that the Finance Committee's review amendment is based on the draft recently sent informally by the Ministry of Finance's Tax Department. The tax rates are all advocated by the Ministry of Finance, not the Finance Committee itself. Chen Guyuan said that this bill should be discussed after the Ministry of Finance sends the official draft to the Yuan. Zhang Zhihan said that the content of this bill still needs to be considered and advocated referring it back for review. Yang Gongda said that the consistent spirit of the Legislative Yuan is to speak from the perspective of the people, and this bill seems to increase the burden on the people. He advocated delaying the discussion. Luo Ding and Lu Zhiyi said that the bill taxes total income without deducting the necessary living expenses of the people, which is unfair. They also advocated referring it back for review. Lin Bin said that there are loopholes in the bill that cause double taxation of the three types of income and seconded the motion to refer it back for review. Although Chen and Liu separately answered the dissenting opinions of the committees, they were outnumbered due to the disparity in power. In addition, Xiao Shuyu, Di Ying, Shi Weihuan, and Wei Tingsheng of the Finance Committee itself were also dissatisfied with the opinions of Chen and Liu. When the chairman put the motion to refer the bill back for review to a vote, it was passed by a vote of 48 to 15. As a result, the chairman designated the Finance and Economic Committees to jointly review the bill with five committee members, Luo Ding, et al. Ma Yinchu convened the meeting and proposed that it be discussed again on the 9th. (Central News Agency dispatch, 7th)

(Nanjing) Ma Yinchu, Chairman of the Finance Committee of the Legislative Yuan, convened a joint meeting of all members of the Finance and Economic Committees and five committee members, Lin Bin, Luo Ding, Lu Zhiyi, Cheng Zhonghang, and Yang Gongda, on the afternoon of the 7th to re-examine the Income Tax Bill. The Ministry of Finance sent Zou Lin, Gao Bingfang, and Liang Jingchun to attend the meeting. Chairman Ma Yinchu passed the amendment to the bill. The number of chapters and articles remained the same. It will be submitted to the special Yuan session on the afternoon of the 9th for review. The main points of the amendment are as follows: The first type of business profit income, which was originally calculated based on the total income as the standard for taxation, is now changed to taxation based on net income. The starting point for taxation of the first type of income, section four, is that income that is 5% to less than 10% of the actual amount of capital will be taxed at 30 per mille. The second type of salary and remuneration income will include the salaries of elementary school teachers in the tax-free scope. In the tax rates for the second type of income, the amount of monthly average income from 31 yuan to 60 yuan will be taxed at 5 fen for every 10 yuan, and the amount from 61 yuan to 100 yuan will be taxed at 1 jiao for every 10 yuan. The rest will remain the same. The third type of securities deposit income will be taxed at a uniform rate of 50 per mille of the income. Foreigners in China will also have to pay income tax according to the law. (Central News Agency dispatch, 7th)

(Nanjing) The draft of the Income Tax Law was submitted to the Legislative Yuan for discussion at the meeting on the 7th. Because most committee members believed that the tax rate was too high, it was decided to refer it back for review. A review meeting was held in the afternoon. Zou Lin, Gao Bingfang, Liang Jing, and others from the Ministry of Finance all attended the meeting to explain the process. It took four hours to complete the review of all the articles. It will be submitted to the General Assembly on the 9th for approval. According to Ma Yinchu, the draft Income Tax Law has been decided to be changed back to the Provisional Income Tax Regulations. It has been reviewed today. The important points of the changes to the original draft are: 1. The original profit income was calculated based on the total amount of profit for taxation, and expenses, etc., were not deducted, which seemed unfair. Therefore, it was revised to calculate taxation based on the net amount of profit. 2. It was decided to add a tax exemption for the salaries of elementary school teachers. Secondary and university teachers will still be taxed. 3. The salaries (from 30 yuan to 60 yuan) will be reduced to a tax of 5 fen for every 10 yuan (originally scheduled to be taxed at 1 jiao). 4. The item (taxing 30 per cent of income that is less than 5 per cent of the total capital) has been deleted to reduce the burden on small businesses. 5. The tax rate to be levied on securities interest income was originally set at 70 per mille, but after review, it was reduced to 50 per mille. These five points of revision were all decided after detailed discussion. As for foreigners in China, it was decided that they will be taxed in the same way. (Special dispatch, 7th)

Contents of the Draft Income Tax Law

(Nanjing) The Legislative Yuan's Finance Committee reported on the review of the draft amendment to the Provisional Regulations on Income Tax, amending the title to the Draft Income Tax Law. The contents are as follows:

Chapter 1: General Provisions. Anyone with one of the following sources of income shall pay income tax in accordance with this law: Category 1: Income from profit-making enterprises: (A) Income from companies, firms, shops, factories, or individuals with capital of more than 2,000 yuan; (B) Income from temporary profit-making enterprises; Category 2: Income from salaries and remuneration: Income from salaries and remuneration of civil servants, freelancers, and others engaged in various occupations; Category 3: Income from securities and deposits: Income from interest on government bonds, corporate bonds, stocks, and deposits. The following types of income are exempt from income tax: 1. Income of legal entities not for profit; 2. Category 2 income: (A) Those with a monthly average of less than 30 yuan; (B) Pensions for military police, officers, soldiers, and civil servants who are injured or killed on duty; 3. Category 3 income: (A) Deposits of government agencies at all levels; (B) Statutory savings of civil servants; (C) Foundation deposits of educational and charitable institutions or groups; (D) Annual interest income from educational savings that does not reach 100 yuan.

Chapter 2: Tax Rates. The tax rates for Category 1, Item A income shall be graded as follows: 1. 30 per mille for income less than 5% of the actual capital; 2. 40 per mille for income equal to 5% of the actual capital but less than 10%; 3. 50 per mille for income equal to 10% of the actual capital but less than 15%; 4. 60 per mille for income equal to 15% of the actual capital but less than 20%; 5. 80 per mille for income equal to 20% of the actual capital but less than 25%; 6. 100 per mille for all income equal to or exceeding 25% of the actual capital. For Category 1, Item B income, the tax rate shall be based on the preceding article if the capital amount can be proportionally determined. If the capital cannot be calculated, the tax rate shall be based on the amount of income as follows: 1. Income less than 100 yuan is exempt from tax; 2. Income of 100 yuan or more but less than 1,000 yuan shall be taxed at 30 per mille; 3. Income of 1,000 yuan or more but less than 2,500 yuan shall be taxed at 40 per mille; 4. Income of 2,500 yuan or more but less than 5,000 yuan shall be taxed at 60 per mille; 5. For income of 5,000 yuan or more, the tax rate shall be increased by 10 per mille for each additional 1,000 yuan. The maximum tax rate for the income in the preceding paragraph shall be 200 per mille. The tax rates for Category 2 income shall be as follows: 1. For monthly average income from 30 yuan to 100 yuan, tax 1 jiao for every 10 yuan; 2. For monthly average income exceeding 100 yuan to 200 yuan, tax 2 jiao for every 10 yuan; 3. For monthly average income exceeding 200 yuan to 300 yuan, tax 3 jiao for every 10 yuan; 4. For monthly average income exceeding 300 yuan to 400 yuan, tax 4 jiao for every 10 yuan; 5. For monthly average income exceeding 400 yuan to 500 yuan, tax 6 jiao for every 10 yuan; 6. For monthly average income exceeding 500 yuan to 600 yuan, tax 8 jiao for every 10 yuan; 7. For monthly average income exceeding 600 yuan to 700 yuan, tax 1 yuan for every 10 yuan; 8. For monthly average income exceeding 700 yuan to 800 yuan, tax 1.2 yuan for every 10 yuan; 9. When the monthly average income exceeds 800 yuan, the tax shall be increased by 2 jiao for every 10 yuan for every 200 yuan exceeded, up to a maximum of 2 yuan for every 10 yuan. If the amount exceeding the monthly income is less than 5 yuan, the exceeding part shall be exempt from tax. If it is 5 yuan or more, it shall be calculated as 10 yuan. The tax rate for Category 3 income shall be 70 per mille.

Chapter 3: Calculation and Reporting of Income. The method for calculating the amount of income is as follows: 1. The income of Category 1 shall be calculated based on the total amount of profit; 2. The income of Category 2, whether calculated monthly or annually, shall be calculated on a monthly average basis. For income that is not regular or is temporary, the income for each month shall be used to calculate the tax; 3. The income of Category 3 shall be calculated based on the interest paid each time it is decided or settled. For Category 1, Item A income, the taxpayer shall report the total amount of income to the competent collection authority in the prescribed format within three months after the end of each year. For Category 1, Item B income, the person withholding income tax or the person paying income tax themselves shall report the total amount of income to the competent collection authority in the prescribed format within one month after the end of the settlement. For Category 2 income, the person withholding income tax or the person paying income tax themselves shall report the total amount of income to the competent collection authority in the prescribed format according to the tax payment deadline. For Category 3 income, the person withholding income tax or the person paying income tax themselves shall report the total amount of income to the competent collection authority in the prescribed format within one month after the interest is paid or received. If the competent collection authority discovers any false concealment or failure to report within the time limit in the income report, it may determine the amount of income.

Chapter 4: Investigation and Review. After the income amount of each category has been reported by the reporting obligor, the competent collection authority may send personnel to investigate at any time. After the competent collection authority determines the amount of income of each category and the amount of tax payable, it must notify the taxpayer. If the taxpayer does not agree with the notification in the preceding paragraph, they must state the reasons and submit supporting documents within 20 days to request the local competent collection authority to conduct a reinvestigation. The competent collection authority shall immediately send other personnel to review and decide. After the review and decision, the taxpayer shall immediately pay the tax in accordance with the law. If the taxpayer still does not agree with the notice of the reinvestigation decision in the preceding article, they may apply to the review committee for review and decision within ten days. The competent collection authority shall deposit the tax payment for which the review is applied in a local reputable bank. After the review committee makes a decision, the tax shall be refunded or supplemented according to the decision. When the competent collection authority refunds the tax in the preceding paragraph, it shall also refund the interest on the refunded portion. If the taxpayer does not agree with the decision of the review committee, they may file an administrative appeal or lawsuit. The review committee shall be established in cities, counties, or other collection areas. The review committee shall have three to seven members, who shall be unpaid and appointed by the Ministry of Finance from local civil servants, impartial persons, and professional group staff members. The term of office shall be three years. When the review committee meets, the head of the competent collection authority or their representative shall attend the meeting.

Chapter 5: Penalties. If a person fails to report or is negligent in reporting within the time limit, the competent collection authority may impose a fine of up to 20 yuan. If a person conceals or makes a false report, in addition to being fined up to 20 yuan, they may also be referred to the court for a fine of two to five times the amount of tax evaded. If the circumstances are serious, they may also be sentenced to imprisonment or detention for up to one year. If a taxpayer or a person withholding income tax fails to pay the tax within the time limit, the competent collection authority may refer the matter to the court for recovery and impose penalties according to the following provisions: 1. If all or part of the tax amount is overdue for more than three months, a fine of up to 30% of the amount owed shall be imposed; 2. If all or part of the tax amount is overdue for more than six months, a fine of up to 60% of the amount owed shall be imposed; 3. If all or part of the tax amount is overdue for more than nine months, a fine of up to 100% of the amount owed shall be imposed.

Chapter 6: Supplementary Provisions. The detailed rules for the implementation of this law, the organizational regulations of the review committee, and other relevant rules shall be determined by the Ministry of Finance. The date of implementation of this law shall be determined by order. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 7th)

Foreign Trade of the Kwantung Leased Territory and the Smuggling Problem in North China

Sugar and Silk are not all absorbed by the Puppet Manchukuo. Indexes of Exports and Imports Deserve Attention

The Zi Lin Bao's Dalian correspondent reported on June 30th, "The Kwantung Government recently released statistics on foreign trade in the Kwantung Leased Territory, with some noteworthy points. The figures are divided into two columns, one for April of this year and one for January to April of this year. In April, exports increased by 31.5% compared to March, and imports increased by 9.1%. Compared with April of last year, exports in April of this year increased by 93%, and exports decreased by 6.4%. This is because smuggling in North China in April of last year was not as rampant as it is this year. The Japanese claim that goods transshipped from the Kwantung Leased Territory to North China cannot be regarded as smuggled goods. Even if this is credible, it is impossible not to relate the recent prosperity of the Jidong market to the expansion of export trade in the Kwantung Leased Territory. However, it is still interesting to analyze these statistics with timely considerations. Now, let us focus on sugar and silk (although rayon is not specifically marked, it is largely included in the silk category). It should be known that neither of these two items is produced locally, and the Puppet Manchukuo relies entirely on Japanese supply. Therefore, the following indexes of exports and imports deserve special attention, especially the export figures. In the first four months of this year, the Kwantung Leased Territory imported sugar worth 10,853,000 Japanese yen and exported sugar worth 5,229,000 yen, accounting for about half of the imports. This is, of course, the largest transaction for re-exporters. The largest transaction was in April, with imports valued at 4,010,000 yen and exports valued at 3,318,000 yen. Therefore, only 692,000 yen worth of sugar remained for local consumption and storage.

The total number of rayon exports and imports is not mentioned. This is clearly listed in the silk category. Moreover, the Kwantung Leased Territory is a very prosperous place for rayon sales. This is well known. It is now said that the rayon smuggled goods stored in North China are shipped from Dalian. Therefore, it is undoubtedly included in the silk category. Most of the silk imported here seems to be re-exported. In the first four months of this year, silk worth 6,104,000 Japanese yen was imported, and silk worth 5,087,000 yen was exported. Therefore, only 1,017,000 yen remained for local consumption and storage. Most of the silk was exported in April, worth 3,546,000 yen, which is more than double the 1,714,000 yen imported that month. The statistics certainly do not specify the destination of the exported goods. However, in April of this year, the Puppet Manchukuo purchased goods worth 1,061,000 yen from the Kwantung Leased Territory. China purchased goods worth 10,131,000 yen. The Puppet Manchukuo's purchases this month largely included various goods, so the sugar and silk exported from the Kwantung Leased Territory were certainly not all absorbed by the Puppet Manchukuo."

Ambition of the Japanese Textile Industry: Expanding Yarn Factories in China

Decided to Take Tianjin as the Center, Expanding by 330,000 Spindles, Aiming to Seize the Entire Chinese Cotton Yarn Industry

A Tianjin correspondent reports that the South Manchuria Railway (Mantetsu) office in Tianjin has been investigating North China's economy, and most of the work has already been completed. Recently, the North China Economic Development issue, jointly discussed by the Japanese Foreign, Colonial, Agriculture and Forestry, and Army Ministries, has come to the fore. Ambassador Kawagoe brought a plan and will explicitly negotiate with our side, so the work has become tense again. The director of the office, Masao Ota, went to Dalian last week to listen to the instructions of the President of Mantetsu, Matsuoka. He returned to Tianjin a few days ago. At the same time, 30 talented employees of the Economic Department's investigation section of Mantetsu's head office were dispatched to Tianjin within the next week to listen to Ota's command and engage in work, still focusing on mines and cotton production. The North China Economic Survey Group, recently initiated by the Japanese Foreign, Colonial, Agriculture and Forestry, and Army Ministries and organized by Japanese business authorities such as Okura, Mitsubishi, and Mitsui, will have a total of 200 people, including various experts in Japan. They plan to come to Tianjin via Northeast China around July 15th, and conduct surveys of mines, cotton production, waterworks, transportation, and other categories, with Tianjin and Beiping as the center of their activities. All the members of the group will be divided into eight groups in order to proceed quickly. The survey period is scheduled for five weeks to two months. This and the Mantetsu's 담당者 have a corresponding role. After the Tianjin Yarn Factory Yuyuan was sold to the Japanese Kanebo Company in May, the machines are being refitted. Kanebo sent a Japanese named Fukunaga as manager, and it was renamed Yufeng First Branch (Yufeng First Branch is in Shanghai). In addition to the original 70,000 spindles, land in Xiaoliuzhuang was purchased, and construction of the Third Branch is planned to begin in April of next year, with a capacity of 70,000 spindles and 1,000 looms. 2,500 Chinese workers and 1,000 Japanese male and female workers will be hired. Three years later, Xiaoliuzhuang will become an industrial area for Japanese living in China. The new yarn factory planned by Toyo Textile Company in Special Area Four will initially have 50,000 spindles, and will continue to expand in the second and third phases, adding 100,000 spindles within two years. The Yuda Yarn Factory, originally operated by Japanese in Tianjin, has 20,000 spindles, and is now supported by the Dai Nippon Spinning Company, which will expand it to 40,000 spindles. Therefore, three years later, in Tianjin alone, Japanese yarn factories will have 300,000 spindles, totaling nearly 35% of all the spindles owned by state-run yarn factories. The Japanese intend to use the aforementioned factories as a base of activity, so that Tianjin will become the center of Japanese yarn sales in the future, supplying markets in South China, North China, and the puppet Manchukuo, and then monopolizing the entire Chinese yarn industry. Each yarn factory will also focus on fine yarn that our country cannot spin. Japanese merchants will also use diplomatic power to obtain preferential treatment from our government for transporting cotton yarn. Therefore, the Japanese yarn industry is very optimistic about future business, but our country's textile industry in Tianjin is worried about it.

The North China wool weaving industry is also being noticed by the Japanese, who are making every effort to develop it. The plan for the Manchuria-Mongolia Wool Weaving Company to set up factories in Zhangjiakou and Tianjin has recently become more concrete. It is said that its purpose is to buy wool, sort it locally, and then divide it into several types, and use cheap wages in North China to build large-scale textile factories in Zhangjiakou and Tianjin to produce wool, wool blankets, and other wool products. The North China wool weaving market is still in British hands. The Japanese plan to completely replace it within five years, and it can be asserted that British wool products will automatically stop shipping because they will be boycotted. (5th)

Agricultural Warehouse Mortgage Loan in Anhui Province

Loan Amount Limited to 1 Million Yuan, Monthly Interest Rate of 8.5 Per Mille, Calculated Daily

Anqing correspondence: The warehousing and mortgage funds needed by provincial and county agricultural warehouses were previously agreed by the Chinese Farmers Bank, the Bank of China, and the China Agricultural Cooperative Loan Syndicate to be loaned, with staff from the Provincial Government present. The Agricultural Warehouse Management Office drafted nine principles for loans from each bank to agricultural warehouses, which were submitted to and passed by the Provincial Government Standing Committee, and staff were sent to each bank to continue negotiating loan contracts. The terms and conditions of the agricultural warehouse mortgage loan contract concluded between the Management Office and the China Agricultural Cooperative Loan Bank are copied below.

The Management Office sends a formal letter of introduction for the agricultural warehouses under its guidance and organization that need warehousing and mortgage funds for handling warehousing and mortgage loans, and the syndicate will approve the loan only after review. The total amount of the loan is temporarily limited to 1 million yuan, and will be increased as appropriate when the agricultural warehouse business develops. The interest rate on the loan is set at 8.5 per mille per month, calculated daily. The term of the loan is from the date of signing the contract to March 31, 1937, and the principal and interest must be settled in full upon expiration. The investment area of the loan is 24 counties including Fengyang, Nanling, Chaoxian, Wuwei, Wuhe, Lingbi, Qimen, Shitai, Yixian, Jingsui, Xixi, Shexian, Langxi, Guangde, Ningguo, Jingxian, Taiping, Qingyang, Guichi, Tianchang, Quanjiao, Boxian, Fuyang, and Yingshang, with 8 provincial warehouses and 50 county warehouses. The loan is specifically for the funds required by the agricultural warehouses listed in the preceding article for warehousing and mortgage business, and may not be used for any other purpose. The measures for agricultural warehouse mortgage loans shall be formulated by the Management Office and the syndicate. The syndicate allows each agricultural warehouse to overdraw 3,000 yuan for the provincial warehouse and 2,000 yuan for the county warehouse for the convenience of loan at the beginning of the business. The syndicate's investment in mortgage loans is based on the agricultural warehouse mortgage certificate, and the agricultural products mortgaged by farmers are used as collateral at 70% of the current price. The agricultural products mortgaged by each agricultural warehouse are used as the first guarantee for the syndicate's loan, and the Management Office is the responsible guarantor for repayment. If there is a mortgage certificate but no collateral is found, the Management shall be fully responsible. If agricultural warehouses that have been loaned mortgage funds by the syndicate handle the transportation and sales of agricultural products, the syndicate shall undertake the mortgage negotiation. The syndicate's investment in mortgage loans to each agricultural warehouse shall be for a maximum of ten months, but shall not exceed the period stipulated in Article 4 of this contract. The syndicate has the right to audit the business and review the accounts of the loaned agricultural warehouses. The syndicate recommends four auditors, who are commissioned by the Management Office, and their salaries and travel expenses are borne by the Management Office. Any matters not covered in this contract may be amended jointly by both parties. This contract shall be made in duplicate, with the Management Office and the syndicate each holding one copy for good faith. This contract shall be submitted by the Management Office to the Anhui Provincial Government for approval and implementation, and shall become effective after both parties formally sign it. (July 5th)

Recent Construction in Guangdong Province

Central District Expands Rural Center Organization, Department of Education Plans to Establish Provincial Museum

Guangzhou Communication: Fan Dexing, Pacification Commissioner of the Central District of Guangdong Province, in order to relieve unemployed farmers and develop the rural economy, established a Central Rural Experiment Zone in the Yuxia area under Panyu County some years ago. Since its establishment, it has achieved remarkable results. Now, in order to expand this central rural initiative and relieve unemployed people, it has been decided to establish central rural cooperatives in counties with sandy fields. Loans will be borrowed from banks and lent to farmers for cultivation. Personnel have been assigned to prepare for this matter, and it will be implemented soon. According to Commissioner Fan, the establishment of central rural areas in various counties to recruit farmers for cultivation will not only relieve the general unemployed population and increase various types of production, but also take the opportunity to promote rural education and maintain local security. This measure is indeed urgently needed.

The provincial government recently decided to establish a provincial museum to promote cultural construction and increase public knowledge. The planning of the museum was instructed to the Department of Education long ago. According to the Department of Education, the department has drafted an estimate of the start-up costs and preparatory period expenses, and has submitted it to the provincial government for review and approval. Once approved, the department will first hire social celebrities and educational experts as members of the museum's preparatory committee to establish a preparatory committee and begin work. It is expected that the museum will be completed within the 25th year [of the Republic, i.e., 1936].

Price Competition Among Yangtze River Steamers

Wuhu Communication: There are five commercial shipping companies operating on the Yangtze River, including the state-run China Merchants Steam Navigation Company and the privately-run Sanbei Company, as well as the British Taikoo and Jardine Matheson, and the Japanese Nisshin. These companies operate over thirty steamers, sailing upstream and downstream between Shanghai and Hankou, passing through various commercial ports such as Nanjing, Wuhu, and Jiujiang, all fully loaded with passengers and cargo, and their business is booming. However, since the completion of the Nanjing-Wuhu Railway and Highway by the Wuhu Jiangnan Railway Company and the Anhui Construction Department, and the joint passenger and freight transport service with the Nanjing-Shanghai Railway, which is fast and convenient, far surpassing the Yangtze River shipping, Wuhu, conveniently located in the middle of the Yangtze River and historically known as "Central River", the business of the Yangtze River steamers downstream has gradually declined due to the evolution of the times. Competition for survival has become an inevitable trend. China Merchants Sanbei took the lead in eliminating malpractices and adopting new transport methods to make passengers feel less weary during their journey, and their business has shown signs of revitalization. Affected by this, foreign shipping companies have recently increased the sale of fourth-class tickets for poor passengers. The fare from Wuhu to Hankou is 1.7 yuan, and the fare from Wuhu to Shanghai is only 1.2 yuan in order to compete with land transportation. In addition to reducing fares, Nisshin's ships have also used various methods to attract passengers and offer small favors to entice the poor and ignorant. As a result, the number of passengers has increased significantly. Taikoo, due to the need to send the Wenzhou and Yifeng steamers to Shanghai for repairs, has specially dispatched the Wanliu, Wantong, and Jintang steamers to join the Yangtze River service. The Wanliu has already decided to set sail from Shanghai, fully loaded with passengers and cargo, passing through Wuhu and heading upstream.

River Dredging Project Completed

The County Construction Bureau's river dredging project for the 24th year originally planned to dredge 14 river channels, which was approved by the provincial department. Later, due to special circumstances in various districts, they were unable to provide labor, so dredging was selectively carried out. A total of nine river channels were dredged, including the Xin'an Creek in the Third District, the Xin Duqiao market river in the Fourth District, Cai Tingqiao Port, the Sitou River in the Fifth District, the Houshu River in the Sixth District, the Panxu Port and Xuchongqiao Port in the Seventh District, and the Bei Qifang Ham in the Ninth District, totaling 26 kilometers in length and 92,000 cubic meters of earth excavated. The project has now been fully completed, costing more than 7,200 yuan for dam construction, water lifting, and other expenses. Yesterday, Director Zhang telegraphed the provincial department, requesting that a commissioner be sent to Wuxi for acceptance inspection. There are still five river channels that have not been dredged, which will be carried out in next year's plan.

Haizhou Grain Prices Gradually Soaring

Since the lifting of the ban on grain exports in this county, all the unscrupulous merchants have taken advantage of the opportunity of the new wheat harvest to borrow money from banks, buy up large quantities of grain for hoarding, and ship them by train and ship to Dalian, Shanghai, Qingdao, Tianjin, Yantai, and other ports for sale, making a considerable profit. As a result, grain prices in Xinpu have soared recently, with wheat selling for around 1.7 or 1.8 yuan per dou (unit of dry measure) in national currency. Poor residents are crying out in misery, and there is great panic about the problem of livelihood.

Ningbo Dongdu Central Fire

The Dajin Shoe Store at No. 10 Dongdu Road in this port, which is solely owned by Zhang Chuxing from Jiangshan, Yin County, was purchased for 8,000 yuan three years ago. It is a three-story, double-opening Western-style facade. At about 1 a.m. this morning, a fire broke out on the third floor. After Zhang discovered it, he immediately took his wife and children and woke up the apprentices to escape. It was extinguished after half an hour. The first and second floors and the facade were fortunately preserved. The store has fire insurance of 9,500 yuan, and the loss is estimated at 4,000 yuan. The neighboring Meili Xiang Clock Shop and Yun Zhang Silk Shop, although their buildings were unscathed, their goods were damaged by water.

Bandit Party Resists Arrest and Engages in Fierce Battle
