Recently, three cases of kidnapping occurred in Zonghan Township within two days. County Magistrate Lin then ordered Hu Guichuan to return to Andong to investigate and arrest them. Unexpectedly, the rioters were aware of this and, due to deep-seated hatred, intended to retaliate. After investigating that they would definitely pass through Gao Wang Road, they gathered more than twenty bandits and ambushed them to wait. Hu Guichuan and more than ten detectives set off in two groups. Detectives Shao Mingcan and others returned to Andong via Gao Wang. When they arrived, the ambushers suddenly emerged, and the gunshots were like a continuous string of pearls. Shao and others immediately returned fire in self-defense. The disparity in numbers was too great, and the situation was extremely critical. Fortunately, the Tianyuan City Security Corps heard the alarm and rushed to the rescue, and the siege was lifted. Both sides reported injuries. County Magistrate Lin, upon hearing the news, immediately ordered the Linshan Security Corps to rush to encircle and suppress them.

A Pleasant Anecdote of the Southern Tour

— Special Correspondent Shi Ying of this newspaper

Impressions of West Lake

The beauty of the scenery of West Lake in Hangzhou, and the secludedness of its mountains, forests, springs, and rocks, have been the subject of countless poems and essays by literati since ancient times. The water, the pagoda, the broken bridge, and the ancient temples each possess a unique style that attracts people and inspires contemplation. Such a landscape is truly as Mr. Kang Youwei said, "Having traveled all over the four continents, I have never seen it."

This time, the reporter's southern tour passed through Hangzhou, and only made a partial visit to West Lake. I hired a small rowboat and first negotiated with the boatman about the places that could be visited in a day, which included Three Pools Mirroring the Moon, Viewing Fish at Flower Harbor, Jingci Temple, Yue Fei Temple, Lingyin Temple, Su Causeway, Huxin Pavilion, Gushan, Lin Bu's Tomb, Fanghe Pavilion, Qiu Jin's Tomb, and more than ten private estates. Other scenic spots such as Feilai Peak, Wuyun Mountain, Longjing Mountain, and Nine Creeks and Eighteen Streams are too numerous to mention, and even visiting for ten and a half months may not be enough to see everything. Therefore, I did not climb or visit them. In fact, visiting strange places and traveling mountains and rivers, the visual experience is certainly not shallow, but the mood can easily feel dull. Although there are many famous attractions that were not visited on this tour, I felt a sense of leisurely fascination and an image created by the heart, and did not feel regret.

Among the various scenic spots visited, several places left a deep impression and are worth mentioning in particular.

Walking to the northern end of the Su Causeway, with its "willows planted between peach trees", is the Yue Fei Temple at the north bank of Yuehu Lake, under Qixia Ridge. Its atmosphere of loyalty and heroism adds a lot of color to the lake and mountains. The temple's solemn and magnificent appearance surpasses all the ancestral halls and temples on the lake. The main hall enshrines the statue of Yue Fei, inscribed "Song Shao Bao Yue Zhongwu Wang" (Prince Yue of Zhongwu, the Junior Guardian of Song). The rear hall enshrines Yue Fei's parents, with Yue Fei's wife and daughter Yin Ping and son-in-law Zhang Xian, and also enshrines five sons and five daughters-in-law. Yue Fei's tomb is on the west side of the main hall, with Yue Yun buried next to him. There are no ancient cypresses as dense as those in the Confucius Forest, nor is there a tomb hall built in the style of the Sun Yat-sen Mausoleum, but the feeling of solemn respect is still the same.

Among the trees at the tomb, there is a cypress tree that was split by lightning, and there is also a pavilion preserving several sections of "Petrified Cypress of Loyal Heart," which makes the sound of metal and stone when struck. It is said that the former is a symbol of the dismemberment of the traitor Qin Hui, and the latter is caused by the accumulation of Yue Fei's loyalty. During the Ming Dynasty, someone added bronze statues of Qin Hui, his wife, Wan Qihai, and Zhang Jun, tied up and kneeling dozens of steps away from the tomb platform. Now they have been replaced with iron statues because tourists constantly spit and curse them, or throw stones at them. The police have issued a prohibition, but it is still difficult to control. The sorrowful and dejected faces of those iron statues seem somewhat ridiculous and pitiful, but when I think back to the events when Qin Hui and his wife sat on a boat on the lake and colluded with the wax pill-selling spy Hami Shi to make a traitorous plan to the Jin people, I even want to hit them with stones, even though I know this is an unconscious act.

In Yue Wumu's hometown of Tangyin County, there is still a reliable story circulating. In the year after the Qing Dynasty fell, a new county magistrate went to Tangyin to take office. He hired a mule driver along the way to carry his luggage. It was winter, the nights were long and the days were short. Before arriving at the city, it got dark and they stayed at an inn. The county magistrate's attendant bought wine under the lamp and invited the mule driver to drink together. In the conversation, the mule driver asked about the county magistrate's surname. The attendant told him that his surname was Qin. The mule driver suddenly turned red in the face and asked urgently, "Is that the Qin of Qin Hui?" The attendant replied, "That's right!" The mule driver pushed away the table and chairs, stamped his feet and slammed the table, cursing, "Today, I, with the surname Yue, am working for the descendants of a traitor, I am truly blind!" After saying that, he turned around, took the mule, and left. The attendant could not catch up and directly told the county magistrate. The county magistrate was initially angry when he heard this, but after thinking about it, he was secretly amazed.

From this perspective, anyone who betrays national interests and is willing to be a clear or secret traitor not only creates iron statue qualifications for themselves, but also smears the faces of their descendants for generations. Contemporary traitors such as Yin Rugeng, Puyi, Zheng Xiaoxu, and "quasi-traitor" Xiao ×× and others, when they think about it in the quiet of the night, should be ashamed and sweating profusely. In that vast sea of suffering, please quickly turn back to avoid casting more iron statues in the future and further staining the jade-like color of West Lake.

The natural scenery of West Lake is inherently beautiful and lovely, combined with the songs of hermits and literati, and the embellishment of chivalrous and loyal souls, thus receiving an even more beautiful reputation. But people's psychology of pursuing and worshiping the spiritual decorations of West Lake, such as ancient tombs, famous ancestral halls, and bronze statues, roughly contains a progressive sense of the times. For example, from the Song to the early Yuan Dynasty, foreign forces expanded, the people suffered, and scholars who were keen on wealth and vanity still had to shamelessly ask their licentious superiors for official positions. Therefore, they felt that Lin Hejing, with his wife of plums and cranes, was commendable for his purity. At the same time, the Song Dynasty imperial family declined, and the Liao and Jin repeatedly launched large-scale invasions. The late Ming Dynasty was also threatened by the Manchu Qing, and both lacked capable generals to resist. Generals like those in Yue Fei's army and Yuan Chonghuan were successively framed by traitors, resulting in their premature deaths before their great ambitions were fulfilled. Therefore, it was felt that Yue Wumu, who sacrificed for loyalty and defending the country, was indeed a standard model soldier of a declining era, and deep respect was paid to him unintentionally. By the late Qing Dynasty, with the rise of revolutions in various places and the success of the Northern Expedition, the general gaze of worshiping martyrs shifted to Xu Xilin and Qiu Jin's chivalrous souls, and the buildings such as Chen Qimei's bronze statue and the Northern Expedition Martyrs Memorial Tower. Today, with the loss of the Northeast and the worsening situation in North China, tourists are moved by the scenery and feel a sense of reverie. Some still cannot help but recall Yue Wumu's military exploits to express the imagination of "returning our rivers and mountains", or even deduce Wumu's saying that "civil officials do not love money, and military generals are not afraid of death", believing that to adapt to the needs of the times, the spirit of "not loving money" and "not fearing death" should be possessed by both civil and military officials. Some ideals are more progressive, assuming that similar memorial buildings will be built in the future, they should not repeat the memorial towers of the Northern Expedition or the Southern Expedition, but should be great victory monuments of the liberation of the Chinese nation and the liberation of the oppressed people of the world.

On the lakeside is a private estate built by a Cantonese person. The magnificence of the buildings and the preciousness of the internal exhibits can probably rival those of other private estates. There is a family ancestral hall here, inscribed "Lake and Mountain Support," which can be said to be extremely grand. Outside the ancestral hall, a separate area is opened up as the cemetery for the estate owner and his nine wives. It is said that the estate owner had served as the prefect of Hangzhou during the Qing Dynasty, and has only been dead for two or three years. Among the wives, there are still some who have not died, only occupying empty tombs. In addition, there are three very young ones (twelve in total), one of whom is afraid of having an empty tomb, and two of whom have already "fled away." The altar, pond, and flowers and trees in the cemetery are so beautiful that even Yue Fei's tomb cannot compare. This is not to belittle Yue Fei's tomb, but to admire the estate owner's ability to make money while serving as the prefect, which is probably not weaker than what officials today call "doorway economics"!

The political center of gravity in Chinese history has mostly been in the north, in order to control Manchuria and Mongolia externally and rule Jiangnan internally. However, Jiangnan's abundant resources hold the lifeline of the economy. Since the Sui and Tang dynasties, the economic advantages of Jiangsu and Zhejiang have gradually risen, forming an important economic center of China. The mountains and rivers of Suzhou and Hangzhou have both innate beauty and acquired superior economic background, adding embellishments and modifications, and have become a scenic area for high-level enjoyment. In fact, Hangzhou is known as a Buddhist land, with temples all over the mountains, attracting a wider range of people and a particularly high reputation. However, while many tourists happily chant the beautiful line "Above is heaven, below are Suzhou and Hangzhou," they should also remember the warning "Do not go to Xinjiang when old, do not visit Suzhou and Hangzhou when young." Looking at the political situation from the Eastern Han Dynasty to the Ming and Qing dynasties, has anyone who came to Jiangnan not been corrupted? The Qing Emperor Qianlong's southern tour was so lingering that he forgot to return. Emperor Yang of Sui built dragon boats and traveled to Yangzhou, until he lost his empire. In fact, the Southern Song Dynasty settled in Hangzhou, and during that period of one hundred and fifty-six years of partial security, their emperors and ministers still drove dragon boats every day, wandering on the lake, calling for palace women to sing and dance incessantly, indulging in pleasure. At that time, the patriotic writer Wen Jiweng's poems and lyrics, "Looking back at the flower world of Luoyang, the land of millet and separation is vast, and there is no more weeping at the New Pavilion. Clusters of happy red makeup shake painted boats, who are the ones who strike the oars in the middle of the river? The hatred of thousands of years, when will it be washed away?" were ignored, but Liu Yong's praising lines, "Three Autumn Cassia, Ten Mile Lotus Fragrance" aroused the ambition of Jin chief Wanyan Liang to "lead a million soldiers to West Lake and stand on the first peak of Wushan."

However, on the other hand, the glamorous and soft beauty of West Lake can easily make people drunk, demoralized, and discouraged. But if people can deeply understand the seriousness of the national crisis and not be indulged by external temptations, the lake and mountains will have their own true colors. How can they be responsible for the loss of the country? Looking at King Goujian of Yue, who slept on firewood and tasted gall, he also rose from the beautiful landscape of Zhejiang to revive his country and seek revenge.

Jiangsu-Zhejiang Railway Bondholders' Group Opposes Railway Ministry's Measures

Submitting requests to the Executive Yuan and Ministry for full payment of principal and interest; Zhejiang General Chamber of Commerce sends telegram requesting remedial measures.

Xin Xin News Agency reports: The Ministry of Railways, in order to settle the previous Jiangsu-Zhejiang Railway bonds, has specifically allocated 800,000 yuan from the completed Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway loan as a one-time complete settlement. The Jiangsu-Zhejiang Railway Liquidation Office has announced that payments will begin on the 6th. The Jiangsu-Zhejiang Bondholders' Group opposes this settlement by the Ministry of Railways, which involves repaying half the principal without interest, causing significant losses to the bondholders. The Zhejiang General Chamber of Commerce has specifically telegraphed the Executive Yuan requesting remedial measures. Details are recorded as follows:

Bondholders' Group Announcement

In addition to telegraphing the Executive Yuan for relief, the Jiangsu-Zhejiang Railway Bondholders' Group issued a notice to all bondholders, stating: "On July 6th, newspapers in this city published announcements from the Ministry of Railways and the Jiangsu-Zhejiang Railway Share Liquidation Office stating that overdue final-term bond payments for the Jiangsu-Zhejiang Railway will be settled by allocating 800,000 yuan from the completed Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway loan, with a discounted one-time repayment. In short, this means repaying half the principal without interest. We are deeply shocked and dismayed. Bondholders purchased these bonds at face value with their hard-earned money, motivated by patriotism and support for the railway. Now, after eighteen years of overdue principal and interest, the accumulated interest has been lost, and the losses are already considerable. For over ten years, bondholders have sent numerous documents and telegrams, but they have been ignored. The nation's credit has been disregarded, and we are deeply saddened. Now, the legally acquired bonds and the owed funds are being repaid with half the principal and no interest, which is even more unjust. The Jiangsu-Zhejiang Railway (now the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway) is generating substantial annual profits. The government profits, and employees receive bonuses, yet the long-overdue principal of the bondholders is being discounted and repaid without interest. We believe all bondholders will find this unacceptable. In addition to telegraphing the Executive Yuan for relief, requesting full payment of principal and interest, we are publishing this announcement to urge all bondholders to unite and advocate for their rights. We also hope that bondholders will postpone redeeming their bonds until full principal and interest are paid, to protect their rights. Deepest hopes." Correspondence address: Room 224, 4th Floor, 441 Hankou Road, Shanghai.

Zhejiang General Chamber of Commerce Telegram

The Zhejiang General Chamber of Commerce of this city telegraphed the Executive Yuan and the Ministry of Railways in Nanjing, stating: "Today's newspaper reported the Ministry of Railways and the Zhejiang Railway Share Liquidation Office's announcement of a discounted repayment plan for overdue final-term share principal and interest and overdue principal and interest on Zhejiang Railway Company bonds. Bondholders Yang Qicheng, Wang Weide, Chen Shenxing, Jin Ruishi, and others came to the Chamber and stated that these stocks and bonds have been overdue for seventeen or eighteen years. According to the legal interest rate, bondholders' losses are already considerable. They hoped for interest to be paid and returned to alleviate their situation. Now, not only is there no interest, but only half of the original face value of the principal and interest is being repaid. The bondholders find this unacceptable, and the share liquidation was approved without consulting the bondholders, which is inappropriate. Please forward this and strongly advocate for a resolution. This case concerns not only credit but also the fact that the Zhejiang Railway has annual profits and substantial gains. These bondholders were key contributors to the initial establishment and maintenance of the railway. It is unfair and unreasonable to leave them with regret. We should remember the source when drinking water. We are reporting this situation and respectfully request you to quickly devise remedial measures to avoid leaving a weakness in the future history of railways." Respectfully, Zhejiang General Chamber of Commerce, Yu.

Japanese Merchants Buying Miscellaneous Grains

Wheat, rapeseed, rice, and other grains have already been loaded for export; the quantity is still small, so the people's food supply is not expected to be affected.

Regarding the matter of Japanese merchants purchasing miscellaneous grains in our country, a Xin Sheng News Agency reporter interviewed Mr. Gu Xinyi, a leader in the grain industry, yesterday and received detailed information, which is recorded below:

Purchasing Miscellaneous Grains

Japanese merchants are purchasing rapeseed in Wuhu and shipping it to Japan for oil extraction. This is a normal occurrence because Japan lacks rapeseed and purchases it from our country every year. As for wheat, they have purchased over 20,000 dan in Wuhu and over 70,000 dan in Shanghai through the exchange, totaling 100,000 dan. At the same time, they have purchased 10,000 bags of rice in the interior, which have been shipped out one after another. It is said that the rice is being shipped to Dalian.

Small Quantity

Japanese merchants usually order wheat from abroad. This year, due to the pricing of foreign wheat, which is higher than our country's wheat, they have changed their policy and purchased it from our country. The quantity of wheat and rice purchased and shipped out is still small, so it is not expected to affect our country's food supply. If Japanese merchants were to purchase a large quantity, it would inevitably cause a shortage and panic in our country's food supply during this period of seasonal scarcity, and at the same time, it would raise the price of rice and other grains, which would affect the livelihood of our people.

Flour Exchange Brokers Hold Emergency Meeting Yesterday

Decide to Revise New Regulations

Shen Shi News Agency reports: Due to the scarce supply of new wheat this year, the poor harvest in the United States, the improvement in the flour market in North China, and the purchase of flour by Japanese merchants, the price of flour has been rising frequently in recent days, and the trading volume has broken the highest record in recent years. The Ministry of Industry and the Bureau of Social Affairs, concerned about the soaring flour prices and their impact on the people's food supply, specifically questioned the Flour Exchange, stating that the recent market situation has deviated from normal business practices and instructed the Exchange to automatically improve its business plan to maintain the people's food supply.

Gu's Advice

To avoid danger, the Exchange suspended trading again yesterday and convened an emergency meeting of all brokers in the afternoon. First, Mr. Gu Xinyi, the director of the Exchange, earnestly advised all brokers and offered the following suggestions: 1. Limit the price; the price on the 6th should be determined by a compromise method to balance the profits and losses of both buyers and sellers. 2. Stop trading in North China wheat immediately. 3. Advise bulls to sell to reduce the trading volume. 4. If there is no solution at the last minute, settle all prices. This measure is unfavorable to the Exchange, and it is best not to implement it. All brokers agreed with the principles of Gu's four suggestions.

Revise New Regulations

Then, the brokers exchanged opinions and discussed countermeasures. After deliberation, the following temporary measures were agreed upon: 1. It was decided to limit the maximum price; the prices for July, August, September, and March were set at 3.05 yuan, and 0.03 yuan was added to each month thereafter, i.e., 3.08 yuan for October, 3.11 yuan for November, and 3.14 yuan for December. 2. Stop new trading immediately. Both new regulations will be submitted to the Bureau of Social Affairs for approval. According to inquiries made by reporters to the person in charge of the Exchange, rumors that the Exchange would add capital and change the chairman of the board are not true. After the new regulations are set, the market price can be stabilized, and there will be no more drastic changes that affect the people's food supply. Trading may resume as usual today, and the chaotic state of the market in recent days can be cleared away.

Shanghai Public Security Bureau Issues Warning Letters to Residents and Shops Regarding Reporting Opium Smokers

To urge landlords and shop managers to pay attention and report unregistered households and shop employees who smoke opium.

To urge landlords and shop managers to pay attention and report unregistered households and shop employees who smoke opium.

The Shanghai Public Security Bureau, in order to strictly report opium smokers and ensure comprehensive registration, has drafted measures for residents to sign pledges and submitted them to the Municipal Government for approval. The Bureau has also issued a type of warning letter to residents and shops to urge landlords and shop managers to pay attention and promptly report unregistered households, shop employees who smoke opium, unregistered opium smokers, and tenants or shop employees who transport and sell opium. The original text of the warning letter is recorded below: "The deadline for reporting opium smokers and registering in this city will be August 10th. After this deadline, opium smokers will no longer have the opportunity to register or voluntarily quit. The Bureau will strictly investigate and confiscate the hidden places of private opium smokers and drug offenders. Landlords and shop managers, if you discover that there are unregistered opium smokers, people who use strong drugs, or tenants or shop employees who secretly transport and sell opium in your co-residents or shops, you should quickly report them to the Bureau, the local police on duty, or submit a letter to the Bureau. If the report is found to be true, we will keep it strictly confidential and apply for a reward in accordance with the regulations. If you conceal the facts and fail to report, you will be held jointly liable if you are discovered in the future. It will be too late to regret it then. We hope that citizens will quickly realize this responsibility and actively report. This is a special warning."

Zhejiang Sericulture and Silk Textile Committee Controls Summer Cocoon Prices

Borrowing Money to Purchase and Reel Over 7,000 Dan of Cocoon Silk for Overseas Sales Through the Sales Promotion Committee

The Zhejiang Sericulture and Silk Textile Committee borrowed 5 million yuan from the Bank of China and Bank of Communications to purchase spring cocoons. The Cocoon Purchasing Committee purchased 110,000 dan (market weight) of improved breed fresh cocoons, equivalent to 30,000 dan (Sima weight) of dried cocoons. The Silk Reeling Committee handed these over to Hangzhou Silk Mill No. 1, Jiaxing Weicheng Silk Mill, and Tangxi Chongyu Silk Mill for reeling, totaling over 7,200 dan of silk. The Sales Promotion Committee is responsible for selling the silk and has already released futures. Over 70 or 80 dan have already been delivered. The current price of Chinese silk in the European and American markets is 650 yuan (Chinese currency) for 20-22 denier silk, slightly higher than when the cocoons were purchased. The Zhejiang Sericulture and Silk Textile Committee has decided to continue controlling summer cocoons. In addition to registering manufacturers who purchase and reel silk, they have also set standard prices for summer cocoons. It has been stipulated that for improved breeds, based on the Sima weight conversion of fresh cocoons at 600 jin (market weight) per reel, the price is 21.11 yuan. For native breeds, based on the Sima weight conversion of fresh cocoons at 660 jin (market weight) per reel, the price is 16.97 yuan. All cocoon merchants who purchase summer cocoons must follow these standard prices.

Office of the China Aviation Association Shanghai Corps Commander Holds 66th Office Meeting

The Office of the China Aviation Association Shanghai Municipal Micro-Request Corps Commander held its 66th Office Meeting at its office at 2:00 PM the day before yesterday (the 6th) to discuss the fundraising progress and direction. Attendees included Chief Secretary Li Dachao, Secretaries Zhu Shengyang, Liu Songtao, Chen Shuo, Li Jiming, Song Zheng, Huang Jun, Gu Shangrui, Li Huiran, Zhang Peihu, Lu Zhangyan, and Wei Jianxin. The meeting was chaired by Li Dachao and recorded by Chen Shuo. The chairman reported that the fundraising efforts to purchase aircraft for birthday congratulations have been promoted diligently by all sectors and organizations in Shanghai, and the results are excellent. The Association previously dispatched special personnel to various important organizations to discuss and facilitate progress, in order to improve the performance of each organization and complete their mission as soon as possible. The progress has been very smooth, and results are being reported and submitted successively. In order to concentrate efforts and promote publicity, a meeting was convened on the 4th with all the ward chiefs in the city to discuss the fundraising efforts for purchasing aircraft for birthday congratulations. The ward chiefs from each district enthusiastically participated, demonstrating the citizens' support for expanding the aviation patriotism movement and their love for the leader. It was resolved that each ward chief would receive a triplicate receipt book to solicit donations from relevant parties, with a minimum of 50 yuan per person, for a period of two months, starting on July 15th. Many people took receipt books after the meeting. Those who did not attend that day have been notified separately and all district property owners have been notified to actively donate and contribute to the fundraising effort for purchasing aircraft for birthday congratulations to facilitate progress. The income from the summer entertainment horse races held by the Shanghai Race Club at Yinxinggang will be transferred as a donation. Mr. Du Yuesheng and the club's enthusiastic support are deeply appreciated. Unfortunately, the results were not satisfactory due to the rain that day. The club has expressed its intention to hold another day, which shows their enthusiasm. The greyhound track (Canidrome) and Jai Alai stadium are raising funds for the aircraft purchase campaign, and Mr. Du Yuesheng is being consulted for assistance, and negotiations are underway, which should be completed soon. The issue of collecting aviation patriotism funds from the sand and gravel industry and the yellow sand crushing industry has been resolved and will begin on July 1st. These industries have united to support the solicitation and fundraising efforts, and the results are excellent. The fundraising situation in other industries is also very good. The external affairs secretaries then reported on the liaison and inspection process, and various fundraising proposals were discussed, and the meeting adjourned at 4:30 PM.

The Commemorative Aircraft Purchase Association has received additional donations sent by the Shanghai Local Association totaling 2,075 yuan, including: Du Yuesheng 1,000 yuan, Lu Runquan 200 yuan, Guo Shun 200 yuan, Zhu Doushan 200 yuan, Zhu Rushan 200 yuan, Zhu Yinjiang 100 yuan, Yu Yefeng 100 yuan, Hua Runquan 20 yuan, Zhang Yixu 20 yuan, Yan Esheng 20 yuan, Jin Lu 5 yuan, Xu Zhiyi 20 yuan, Jin Zhixuan 20 yuan, Ren Jisheng 10 yuan, Xu Qiufan 10 yuan, and Pan Xulun 50 yuan. More funds are being collected and will be submitted later. Captain Zhu Jingan raised 1,000 yuan from the Shanghai Ningbo Association, 23.2 yuan from the Postal Savings Bureau, and 200 yuan from the International Trade Bureau. Mr. Zai Boji raised 123 yuan (Japanese currency) from the crew members of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company Huashan Steamer. Mr. Gu Yuqi donated 100 yuan, the students of Ai Qiu Primary School donated 13.6 yuan, and the Datong Dyeing and Weaving Factory donated 10 yuan. All have been received and thanked.

Yunnan Sanyi Plant Oil Refinery Requests

Joining the China Plant Oil Factory

Ministry of Industry Directs Preparatory Office to Deliberate Carefully

Yunnan Province is located in a remote border region with difficult transportation, but the province's rich products have long been known to the world. The province's agricultural products, in addition to rice, include soybeans, grape seeds, rapeseed, tobacco seeds, perilla seeds, and other seed materials, which are the most common raw materials for oil extraction. Other trees, such as tung trees, lacquer trees, and Toona sinensis trees, are nearly everywhere in the areas of Qiaojia, Yiliang, Yongshan, and Zhenxiong in eastern Yunnan. Taking tung seeds as an example, the oil extracted each year, in addition to being used as fuel, is transported out from Bijie, Yongning, and Yibin in quantities of hundreds of thousands of catties. However, the traditional methods of production are used, with impurities mixed in, incomplete refining, and impure quality and color. There is no standard for refining, which has a significant impact on health, food, industrial products, and other uses. The authorities have not paid attention, and the people have not improved. Therefore, local business leaders raised capital of 500,000 Yunnan dollars in the 18th and 19th years of the Republic (1929-1930) to establish the Sanyi Plant Oil Refinery Co., Ltd. They purchased three mu of land on the east bank of the Desheng Bridge River and built Western-style factory buildings. They ordered a complete set of new-style 16-horsepower knife pressing oil extraction machines from the French Olier Factory, including four oil pressing machines, oil filtering machines, seed crushing machines, and seed roasting machines, as well as a steam boiler, an electric generator, and oil storage tanks and warehouses. The scale is grand. The equipment was completed in October of that year and oil extraction began. The factory can process 1,600 catties of seeds and produce 500 catties of pure oil in 10 hours of work per day. The products include "Caiflower Brand" red seed oil (i.e., grape seed and black seed oil, i.e., rapeseed), raw oil, and white seed oil (i.e., tobacco seed oil). Plans have also been made to process tung seeds from Qiaojia counties when the highway is completed and transportation becomes convenient this winter. Since the sale of the above products, they have been warmly welcomed by people from all walks of life. They are considered the best hygienic product for vegetarians and are happily purchased. Supply cannot meet demand. The Yunnan Product Appraisal Conference awarded the factory a special award certificate, and the Yunnan Construction Department and the Municipal Government registered and approved the factory to be tax-exempt. Recently, the factory heard that the Ministry of Industry, together with Sichuan, Hubei, Hunan, Anhui, Zhejiang, and other provinces, is initiating the organization of a China Plant Oil Factory, and it strongly agrees. Therefore, it specifically submitted a report to the Ministry of Industry, requesting the dispatch of personnel to the Yunnan factory for inspection and takeover, converting it into a branch factory, or adding equity capital for joint government-business operation. The Ministry of Industry has instructed the preparatory office of the China Plant Oil Factory to deliberate carefully on the cooperation methods.

Shanghai Yearbook to be Published Soon

Rich in Content, Double that of Last Year; New Materials, Convenient Reference

The 25th edition of the Shanghai Yearbook has long been compiled by the Shanghai Local History and Newspaper Office. Its content is richer and more accurate than the first edition last year, and reference is particularly convenient. If you want to deposit money, you can check the history and capital of various banks in the financial section of the book. If you want to engage in commerce, you can check the commercial section of the book, such as trade associations. The information on the municipal government is even more detailed. Almost everything about Shanghai can be found in this book. The book is being printed by the Zhonghua Book Company and will be officially published in early August.

Sugihara Takes Over as Acting Japanese Consul-General

Former Japanese Consul-General in Shanghai, Ishizaki Jotaro, has been promoted to envoy to Dhaka and has left Shanghai for his home country. The vacancy of Consul-General has been filled by the senior consul, Mr. Sugihara, as acting Consul-General. It is reported that the Shanghai Municipal Council has received a notification from Mr. Sugihara that he took over as acting Consul-General on the 5th.

Medical Doctor Chen Kehui Returns to Country and Arrives in Shanghai Yesterday

Dr. Chen Kehui, a medical doctor who studied in America and has been the director of the pharmaceutical department of the Eli Lilly pharmaceutical factory for many years, decided to return to his hometown to visit relatives. He set out from Shanghai in mid-last month with his family on the Dollar Line's President Jackson, and arrived in port at 4:30 PM yesterday. Those who came to welcome him at the New Customs Wharf included Dr. Sun Keji, Yang Yujie, the director of the Jiangwan District Health Office of the Bureau of Health, the Shanghai branch manager of Eli Lilly, and friends and relatives of Mr. Chen. He then went to the residence of his younger brother, Mr. Chen Kecheng, to stay temporarily. It is reported that Mr. Chen has been away from the country for a long time, and his medical research abroad has been very successful, so public and private medical groups and individuals in this city have planned a welcome reception for him.

China International Famine Relief Commission Releases Report on Emergency Relief in Western Shandong by Delegation of the Red Cross Society

The China International Famine Relief Commission at 505 Henan Road was previously entrusted by the China Red Cross Society to distribute emergency relief in the four provinces of Hunan, Hubei, Shandong, and Jiangsu. The distribution situation in Hunan, Hubei, and Jiangsu has been recorded in previous reports. Now, we record the report of Mr. Ji Luyi, the distribution staff in Western Shandong: "Luyi was honored to be appointed by the General Association to distribute the funds for the Red Cross Society’s Western Shandong relief, including 10,000 yuan, 2,000 bags of flour, five boxes of medicine, and 21 bundles of large and small clothing, hats, and shoes. In order to know the actual situation in the disaster area in advance, before the distribution, twelve people were dispatched to inspect more than 100 villages in the Wenshang and Jiaxiang area, so as to assess the situation. According to the report, the disaster area was flooded, the soil was loose, and transporting relief supplies was very difficult. Therefore, a relief distribution station was established in the urban area, and 2,000 flour relief tickets and 3,000 clothing relief tickets were distributed to the disaster victims, so that they could bring the tickets to exchange for the goods. At that time, there were many disaster victims suffering from diseases, and medical relief was very necessary. Therefore, 10,000 yuan of relief funds were transferred for medical treatment and medicine distribution, including 9,700 yuan to Jining Hospital and 300 yuan to Yanzhou Hospital. Over the past few months, there have been 4,500 people seeking treatment, and there are still more than 90 people hospitalized. This is the situation of the emergency relief distribution in Western Shandong."

Tan Zhuohong and Yang Shaopeng's Judgment in the Case of Dereliction of Duty

The case of bribery involving judges and lawyers in Shanghai's judicial circles, which caused a great stir, was reported to the Ministry of Judicial Administration. The Ministry secretly ordered the Shanghai District Court Judge Tan Zhuohong and Lawyer Yang Shaopeng to be handed over to the Wuxian District Procuratorate for investigation. Prosecutor Zhu Shufen initiated a public prosecution for dereliction of duty. The Criminal Court President Yu Zhong and Judges Fang Duohuan and Chen Ziguan formed a collegial panel to conclude the trial. The judgment was made on the 25th of last month.

Main Text: Tan Zhuohong is sentenced to eight years of imprisonment and deprived of civil rights for ten years for jointly and continuously soliciting bribes from public officials for actions violating their duties. Yang Shaopeng is sentenced to six years of imprisonment and deprived of civil rights for eight years for jointly and continuously soliciting bribes from public officials for actions violating their duties. After hearing the judgment, both defendants expressed their dissatisfaction and prepared to appeal. The judgment, now delivered, is recorded as follows:

Facts: Tan Zhuohong, serving as a judge in the Shanghai Local Court, and Yang Shaopeng, practicing law in Shanghai, colluded with each other to solicit bribes from parties involved in cases. On October 7, 1935, Tan Zhuohong accepted Zhang Qidong's private prosecution against Song Dacheng for defamation. On June 13, he handled the case of Qin Zhengru, the owner of the Haizhou Steamship Company, causing death by negligence. On September 9, he accepted Lei Yunsheng's lawsuit against Wang Bingnan for counterfeiting trademarks. On October 5, he handled Wu Peizhen's private prosecution against Li Keting for interfering with marriage. On June 28, he accepted Cheng Li Tianzhi's lawsuit against Xu Yi for counterfeiting documents. However, the Qin Zhengru case was mediated by Xi Hanchu, who entrusted Qi Yougen, a steward on the Zhida Steamship, to speak on his behalf. The rest were all handled by Yang Shaopeng, who contacted the parties involved one after another. Regarding the case of handling Wu Peizhen's private prosecution for interfering with marriage, which originally involved a spouse, and therefore could not be privately prosecuted, Tan still accepted it. Moreover, before soliciting a bribe, he detained the defendant Li Keting. In the case of Qin Zhengru causing death by negligence, he leaked the sentence before the judgment. In the case of Wang Bingnan counterfeiting trademarks, he disclosed all the details of the case due to soliciting a bribe. Later, after someone reported it to the Ministry of Judicial Administration, the Ministry secretly ordered the Chief Prosecutor of the Second Branch of the Jiangsu High Court and the Chief Prosecutor of the Shanghai Local Court to investigate and respond. Tan Zhuohong, Yang Shaopeng, and others, along with all the case files, were handed over to the prosecutor of this court for investigation and prosecution.

Reasoning: Whether the defendants Tan Zhuohong and Yang Shaopeng are guilty of the charges in this case should be determined based on whether there is criminal conduct. During the interrogation of Tan Zhuohong and Yang Shaopeng, both denied the fact of jointly soliciting bribes. However, the criminal conduct of the defendants is confirmed by the following points:

(1) Regarding the case of Zhang Qidong, Yang Dingchen, and others privately prosecuting Song Dazheng for defamation, witness Sun Zuji repeatedly testified, "The case was heard for the first time on October 14th of last year. On the 16th, Yang Shaopeng came to my office and said, 'Do you want to find a way to deal with your case? Judge Tan of the Local Court has asked me to contact you. He said that the defendant can be prosecuted, but the plaintiff must pay a considerable price.' I immediately refused and informed the parties involved. Fearing that Judge Tan might have prejudices, I withdrew the private prosecution." Zhang Qidong and others also stated, "The case was heard for the first time on October 14th of last year, and there have been no hearings since. I went to Lawyer Sun's office around October 20th. According to Lawyer Sun, Lawyer Yang Shaopeng came to discuss the case on the 16th of this month, saying that he was Judge Tan, who was handling our case in court, and he asked him to say that our evidence was very weak. If we wanted to prosecute the defendant, we had to pay a considerable price. We refused and said that the defendant had repeatedly failed to appear after being summoned. We requested a warrant for arrest according to the law, but it was not approved. Judge Tan also pointed out in court that the evidence was weak and spoke very harshly." This is consistent with the testimony of witness Chen Fengming, "On October 6th of last year, I went to Sun Zuji's office. Only he and Wang Jiecheng were there. Later, a person came, whose name I did not know at first. Later, Sun Zuji told me that it was Yang Shaopeng. Sun Zuji took out a business card and said, 'What a joke! What a joke!' I asked him what was the matter. He said that he was handling a very small case. The judge of the court asked him to say that the evidence was weak and that if he wanted to prosecute the defendant, he had to pay a considerable price." The statements made by Wang Jiecheng are also consistent. The business card that Sun Zuji submitted to the court, the statements of the witnesses, and the other witness reports mentioned match each other. The fact that defendants Tan Zhuohong and Yang Shaopeng solicited bribes for public officials' actions is provable, and their empty words and excuses cannot absolve them of their criminal responsibility.

Regarding the case of Qin Zhengru, the owner of Haizhou Steamship, causing death by negligence, defendant Tan Zhuohong denied colluding with Xi Hanchu to solicit bribes from the parties involved. However, Wu Zhiquan, the chief mate of Haizhou Steamship, stated, "After the court hearing, a steward on the Zhida Steamship named Qi Yougen came and said, 'Your case needs some money to be spent to avoid trouble. I know a Xi Hanchu. This Gong Hanchu has a relationship with the judge handling the case. He can find a way, and he can even invite the judge to eat together, but not at the same table.' I told Qin Zhengru about this, and he told me to ignore him. Not long after, Qi Yougen said to me again, 'If you don't spend money, the judge is going to sentence you to three years in prison, but it hasn't been announced yet. If you are willing to spend some money, there is still a way.' I refused again. Later, Qin Zhengru was sentenced to three years in prison (on August 21st)." This is completely consistent with the repeated statements of witness Zhu Yisheng. Although Qi Yougen has repeatedly failed to appear after being summoned, the testimony of Zhu Yisheng, the lawyer representing Lei Yunsheng in the case of Lei Yunsheng suing Wang Bingnan for counterfeiting trademarks, can be referenced. He said, "In this case, after Judge Tan held a court session on September 18th of last year, Yang Shaopeng came to my office and said, 'Don't worry about the Qin Zhengru case. Everything is the fault of the one named Gong.'" It can be determined that defendant Tan Zhuohong colluded with Gong Hanchu and leaked confidential information regarding the trial in advance in order to solicit bribes. In a letter from Tan Zhuohong's wife, Tan Li Ruyi, from Guangzhou, it said, "Gong Yu Chen Ru must be careful. You also hate him." Combined with what the old steward Qi Yougen said, "Gong Hanchu has a relationship with the defendant," this can further prove that Gong Hanchu solicited bribes on behalf of the defendant. Furthermore, observing the handling of the case, after Qin Zhengru was sentenced to three years in prison, he appealed to the second instance, and the original judgment was revoked, and Qin Zhengru was declared not guilty. Although the handling of the case involves different legal interpretations, the clues are still traceable. The statements of the witnesses coincide with each other, who can believe that it was not leaking secrets and soliciting bribes?

Regarding the case of Lei Yunsheng suing Wang Bingnan for counterfeiting trademarks, Zhu Yisheng, the lawyer representing Lei Yunsheng in the incidental civil suit, repeatedly stated, "After the court hearing in this case, Yang Shaopeng came to my office soon and said, 'Don't worry about the Qin Zhengru case. Everything is the fault of the one named Gong.' Later, Yang Shaopeng said, 'Now, in the case of Wang Bingnan counterfeiting trademarks, Judge Tan asked me to say that if you spend some money, you can get a satisfactory outcome.' I refused at first. On October 2nd, after the second court session, he called again and asked me to pay 2,000 yuan. I refused again. Soon, he called again and reduced it to 1,000 yuan. Later, he called again and reduced it to 400 yuan. When it was reduced to 400 yuan, it was after the end of the debate on the 18th. He gave you a last chance and reopened the debate. I was very strange about this. Yang Shaopeng revealed the Qin Zhengru case as soon as he opened his mouth, which made me believe that he was sent by Judge Tan. I wondered how Yang Shaopeng knew about the Qin Zhengru case." When questioning Zhao Deru, the business director of Lei Yunsheng, he stated, "After the lawsuit was filed, the criminal court held the first hearing. I went to Zhu Yisheng's office to inquire about the situation. Zhu Yisheng said, 'Yang Shaopeng came and asked us to spend some money on the court. We ignored it because the evidence was solid.'" The details of Zhu Yisheng's statements are consistent, and they are also connected to the facts of Gong Hanchu's statement by Wu Zhiquan. After defendant Tan Zhuohong took over the case, he declared the debate concluded on October 18, 1935, and then reopened the debate on the 27th of the same month. Whether there was a need to reopen the debate is questionable. Moreover, the witnesses who should have been summoned after reopening the debate had not yet fulfilled their duties. And the evidence of him leaking secrets to create opportunities for soliciting bribes is clear. There is no room for further defense.

(4) Regarding the case of Wu Peizhen suing Li Keting for interfering with marriage, the case file shows that Wu Peizhen filed a private prosecution in her capacity as a spouse. The original judge, Lu Hongze, took leave, and defendant Tan Zhuohong took over. Witness Gao Junxiang stated, "The case was heard in October of this year. Judge Tan ordered the defendant to pay a deposit of 1,000 yuan for bail, and then increased it to 10,000 yuan. Soon, Yang Shaopeng came to my office and said, 'Judge Tan is handling this case. There are many attachments to the lawsuit. What are your thoughts?' I was very strange at the time and said that Judge Tan's actions were inexplicable, and I had no opinion. At this time, Lawyer Lu Jiazi came and said that because of the spouse status, a private prosecution could not be filed, and illegally detaining the defendant was illegal." Lu Jiazi then said, "In October of last year, Wu Peizhen sued Li Keting for interfering with marriage. Li Keting first selected Gao Junxiang as his defense lawyer, fearing that Judge Tan, who was handling the case, had disagreements with Gao Junxiang. Later, I was added as a defense lawyer. After accepting the case, I went to Gao Junxiang's office on the 16th or 17th of the same month and saw Yang Shaopeng sitting there. I heard Gao Junxiang say, 'I have no opinion on this matter. Judge Tan's handling of the case is inexplicable.' I immediately said that since I had taken over this case, and since Yang Shaopeng was speaking on behalf of Judge Tan, I told Yang Shaopeng that Judge Tan's illegal detention of the defendant was wrong. I asked Yang Shaopeng to inform Judge Tan not to do such illegal things. The next day, I went to the court to request a hearing. Judge Tan then handed the defendant over to me to take back. Later, Judge Lu ruled that the case would not be accepted." This is consistent with what Gao Junxiang said. When questioned, Yang Shaopeng admitted that he went to Gao Junxiang's office and heard Lu Jiazi say that Judge Tan should not have accepted this case and stubbornly detained the defendant. I immediately called Judge Tan and asked him to refer to the law and handle this case carefully. Tan Zhuohong also stated in court that he was interrogated by you (referring to Yang Shaopeng) over the phone. Thus, he knowingly accepted a case that should not have been accepted, sometimes detaining and sometimes entrusting the defendant. Yang Shaopeng first hinted at soliciting a bribe, and then because Lu Jiazi's words were strong, he notified Tan by phone and then entrusted Li Keting. The situation of their collusion to solicit bribes is extremely obvious. Moreover, as evidenced by a letter from Yang Shaopeng from the detention center of this court to his wife Chen Qinbao, also known as Chen Xiuying, which stated, "Please ask Lawyer He Qi to visit Lawyer Lu Jiazi once and ask him for help. Just say that we happened to meet in Lawyer Gao Junxiang's office, and it was a friendly chat, discussing idle matters. Yang also had no other intentions. Regarding Lawyer Gao Junxiang, my dear wife, go to Lawyer Chen's office with Mr. Zhang Zhaomei and ask Lawyer Chen to speak on my behalf. Please ask Lawyer Gao to say the same thing as Lawyer Lu Jiazi, just saying that Lawyer Yang happened to come to my office to play one day, and everyone was chatting about idle matters, and Lawyer Yang had no other intentions regarding the case, and when he did have an opinion, it was after Lawyer Gao brought it up, and Yang said, 'What is your opinion from a legal standpoint?' and it was without any bad intentions." In this case, the defendants are making excuses for the truth and are attempting to get off lightly; the instructions to his wife suggest this. Moreover, it also says that the pair had no other intentions. If the defendant had not colluded to solicit bribes, why would he ask Lu Jiazi and Gao Junxiang to cover up for him? His heart had already contained ill-doing from the start. Furthermore, the evidence that Lu Jiazi offered to the court suggests his involvement. Lu Jiazi stated, "Yang Shaopeng is a good person, but an honest person is bound to get himself into trouble sometimes." He also said, "Judge Tan's reputation is not very good. His soliciting money has become an open secret. In the cases that have been exposed, he has not yet obtained the money. In the cases where he has already obtained the money, people are afraid of committing crimes and dare not reveal it." Even Lu Jiazi, whom Yang Shaopeng admires, testifies like this, which means that the defendants colluded to solicit bribes, which is already clear. Moreover, Wu Peizhen and Li Keting are spouses, and the Criminal Procedure Law clearly stipulates that they cannot file a private prosecution. The defendant, as a judge, cannot claim not to know this, but he still accepted the case illegally and arbitrarily detained the defendant. This is a violation of his duty. He then colluded with Yang Shaopeng to solicit bribes. The evidence of guilt is clear, so there is no need to explain it further.

(5) Regarding the case of Cheng Li Tianzhi suing Xu Yi for counterfeiting documents, after Tan Zhuohong accepted the case, the plaintiff originally appointed Lawyer Li Shirui as his civil lawsuit representative. Later, due to Li Shirui's introduction, Yang Shaopeng was added as the representative on July 9th, and a fee of 4,000 yuan was agreed upon. Defendant Yang Shaopeng stated, "There are many rumors in Shanghai. They may think that I know Judge Tan, but in fact, it is all official business." He also said, "At that time, the newspaper reported that Xu Yi was sentenced to four months of imprisonment. The victim was represented by me. They thought that I had a relationship with Judge Tan. The rumors were so strong at the time that I was afraid to come to the local court." He refused to admit the fact that he solicited a bribe of 8,000 yuan from Cheng Li Tianzhi and handed it over to Tan Zhuohong. However, a letter signed by the Guangdong Tongyi Association (Yang Shaopeng did not deny the existence of the Tongyi Association in Guangdong in his court testimony) stated, "Yang Shaopeng's actions are indeed illegal, but it must be known that he was passive, and the principal offender is actually Judge Tan Zhuohong of your court's criminal court. Since being appointed as a judge, he has personally contacted Yang Shaopeng at his residence for every case. Sometimes, he would ask Yang to go to the Xiafei Apartment for secret talks in a separate room. The first time he solicited a bribe was in the Xu Yi case, when he asked Lawyer Li to obtain 8,000 yuan from the Cheng family and give it to Tan Zhuohong for expenses." Xu Yi also stated in court, "Judge Tan is very interested in money. Therefore, when trying cases, regardless of the size, the parties involved are often detained by him. If someone (referring to Yang Shaopeng) pleads on their behalf, they can be released on bail." He also said, "Judge Tan lives in the Xiafei Apartment and meets with Lawyer Yang there." These statements are consistent. Although Cheng Li Tianzhi denied the fact that defendant Yang Shaopeng solicited a bribe from him in court, the contract of engagement between Cheng Li Tianzhi and Yang Shaopeng, which this court reviewed, stated that 2,000 yuan would be paid first, and the remaining 2,000 yuan would be paid after a satisfactory judgment. Furthermore, the word "satisfactory" was crossed out. The case is still under trial, and whether Xu Yi is guilty is not yet known. However, Yang Shaopeng was able to use a satisfactory judgment as the object of the contract. This shows that he and defendant Tan Zhuohong colluded with each other, used cases to solicit bribes, and the details are obvious. Furthermore, Yang Shaopeng once said that they thought that I knew Judge Tan, and again that they thought that I had a relationship with Judge Tan. His blatant collusion with Tan Zhuohong to solicit bribes is tantamount to admitting it himself. Furthermore, referring to the points in the letter from Yang Shaopeng to his wife, the letter stated, "The two photos that I showed you in the corner of the Shanghai Local Court were written by that bastard (referring to Tan Zhuohong) to President Luo and President Cai, and the delivery receipt (everything below the writing in the original letter was smeared with ink). I have kept it all along because the thief Tan is untrustworthy. If the thief Tan harms me, I will use it as evidence, and the thief Tan will be in trouble. But don't show it now, so please find it and put it in Shen Fengzao's residence. Do not tear it up. This matter is a matter of life and death. I am afraid that my dear wife has not paid attention to it and has not done it well, so I will mention it again. Because the thief Tan is not human, the thief Tan wants to avoid getting wet himself and wants to accuse me of deception. If he is so unconscionable, my only evidence is the photos mentioned above. Also, in the drawer of the desk in my office, there is also a business card of the thief Tan, with a word on it written by the thief Tan, and a guest list of the thief Tan inviting Shen Fengzao and others to dinner at Dajiali. Please keep them safe and do not put them at home." And in the letter to Zhang Shizhao, it said, "If I do not uphold justice, he (referring to Tan Zhuohong) is really in trouble. His usual behavior is difficult to describe in one word." The defendant said that the thief Tan wanted to harm me, and I will use it as evidence, and the thief Tan will be in trouble; the thief Tan is not human and wants to avoid getting wet himself and wants to accuse me of deception; my only evidence is the photos mentioned above; if I do not uphold justice, he is really in trouble, and his usual behavior is difficult to describe in one word. His usual collusion with Tan Zhuohong to illegally solicit bribes is vividly displayed on paper. The letter was Yang Shaopeng's secret instruction to his wife, trying to eliminate his crimes. He did not expect to be discovered, so his true feelings were revealed unconsciously, and can be adopted. This is especially the most powerful and unique ironclad evidence for confirming the crime. Even if he had a hundred mouths, it would be difficult to defend himself. Furthermore, during the investigation, he entrusted the Shanghai First Special District Local Court to order Yang Shaopeng's wife and Shen Fengzao to hand over the photos and the guest list mentioned in the letter, but Shen Fengzao and others refused to hand them over, which can be definitively said to be evidence of soliciting bribes. Tan Zhuohong denied that he knew Yang Shaopeng well, saying that he only met him at a friend's house. However, judging from the tone of the letter, the defendant's intimacy and collusion with Yang Shaopeng is enough to prove it. Furthermore, when reviewing a business card of Tan Zhuohong found in Yang Shaopeng's home, Yang Shaopeng stated that the word "吾" on the business card was changed by Tan Zhuohong. Comparing it with the handwriting of Tan Zhuohong in court, it is clear that it was written by the same person, which further proves the collusion between Tan Zhuohong and Yang Shaopeng to solicit bribes, and there is no room for sophistry. Based on the above statements and evidence, the guilt of the defendants is clear, and they should be held responsible for their crimes. Their actions constitute the crime of a public official soliciting bribes for actions that violate their duties, knowingly accepting a case that should not be accepted, arbitrarily detaining the defendant, and leaking confidential information. Although Yang Shaopeng does not have the status of a public official, he participated in the actions that constitute the elements of the crime and should still be convicted of the same crime. Their successive actions have different methods of violating their duties, but they are based on a general intention to commit the same type of crime and should be considered as one crime. Furthermore, the crimes they committed are related, so the most severe punishment should be applied. Tan Zhuohong is a judge, and Yang Shaopeng is a lawyer. They should have cultivated integrity and set an example, but they violated the law and neglected their duties, which is unforgivable. Because they are continuous offenders, their sentences should be increased by one-half according to the law. After considering the circumstances, separate sentences should be imposed. The defendants are sentenced to more than six months of imprisonment. Based on the nature of the crime, it is deemed necessary to deprive them of their civil rights, and they are deprived of their civil rights separately. Based on the above conclusions, in accordance with Article 291, Article 292 of the Criminal Procedure Law, Article 28, Article 120, paragraph 1, Article 120, paragraph 1, item 1, Article 132, paragraph 1, Article 56, Article 55, Article 37, paragraph 2, and Article 31 of the Criminal Law, the judgment is as stated in the main text. Prosecutor Zhu Shufen performed his duties in court. June 25, 1936, Criminal Court of the Wuxian District Court of Jiangsu, Presiding Judge Yu Zhong, Judges Fang Qinghuan and Chen Ziguan.

Ningxing Steamer Suspended for Repairs Yesterday

Regular scheduled trip canceled once, passengers temporarily returned

The Ningxing steamer of the Sanbei Company, which is the regular scheduled ship between Shanghai and Ningbo, with sailings from Shanghai on Tuesdays, Thursdays, and Saturdays, also traveling to Zhenhai to load goods from the mainland, entered the port yesterday from Ningbo to Shanghai. It was discovered that the engine wings of the ship were damaged and could not sail. After the shipowner reported to the company, the company sent personnel to inspect the ship's wings and confirmed that they were damaged. If it continued to sail, it would be very dangerous. The company immediately ordered the Ningxing steamer to be opened to the plant for repair. According to the regulations for regular scheduled Shanghai-Ningbo ships, if an accident occurs and the schedule is suspended, a ship must be sent to sail in its place. At that time, there was no equivalent oceangoing ship in Shanghai, so the company had to suspend the ship for one trip and rush to repair the damaged wings in the next day and a half so that it could resume normal operations on Thursday. Passengers were notified, but the passengers did not know and arrived at the ship's wharf in Nanshi yesterday to board the ship and had to return temporarily. Some of them changed to the Xinjingtian steamer to go to Ningbo.

French Concession Public Works Department Stipulates Regulations for Garbage Disposal

The French Concession Public Works Department pays close attention to the issue of garbage disposal. Now is the summer season, and residents should pay particular attention to hygiene and cleanliness. The department has newly revised the regulations for garbage disposal as follows: Each resident should have a lightweight garbage bin with a lid for daily garbage disposal. The department has model garbage bins for sale. Unless otherwise agreed between the department and the property owner, all garbage collectors employed by the department must not enter private residences, private roads, or alleys. Residents should move the garbage bin to the roadside every morning when the garbage truck passes by, and the department's collectors will empty it. If the property owner requests the department's cleaners to sweep the garbage in private roads and alleys, the property owner must pay a handling fee in advance for six months at a time. The fee should be 4% of the total monthly rent of all houses in that area. The garbage truck passing time is as follows: from April 1st to September 30th every year, from 5:00 AM to 8:00 AM; from October to March 35th of the following year, from 6:00 AM to 9:00 AM. Each garbage truck has a ringing bell to alert residents. Anyone who violates these regulations will be fined from one yuan to five yuan. Repeat offenders will be fined double. The following should be noted: the so-called garbage refers to the residue discarded from temples and the dust collected from homes. Leaves from gardens, animal feces, or bricks and soil should not be regarded as garbage and should be transported by the residents themselves. The department specially reminds citizens within the concession to pay attention, knowing that if garbage is disposed of on the road at will, there will be many disadvantages (such as breeding flies and breeding germs). It is hoped that citizens within the concession will abide by the regulations.

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce Commodity Exhibition Hall Thoroughly Investigates the Solicitation of Publications and Advertisements Under False Pretenses

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce Commodity Exhibition Hall was founded in the tenth year of the Republic of China and has been in operation for fifteen years. Every year, it has made unremitting efforts to promote national products. It is found that the exhibition hall had previously edited books such as "National Products Jinliang," "National Products Monthly," "National Products Yearbook," and "Essentials for Industry and Commerce" for the purpose of publicizing national products. Later, the exhibition hall decided that, except for "National Products Jinliang," all other publications would be discontinued and merged into "National Products Jinliang." Therefore, no other publications have been published recently. However, recently, unscrupulous people have been soliciting publication advertisements in the name of the exhibition hall. The exhibition hall has now discovered this and is conducting a thorough investigation. Please pay attention to all sectors of society. If such incidents are discovered again, please detain the person soliciting advertisements and notify the exhibition hall for investigation.

Ma Bosun, the grandson of the famous Jiangwan ENT doctor Ma Fengfu, has a residence at No. 902 Haiphong Road, and has another branch clinic at No. 4, Lane 830, Beijing Road. holding a plantain fan

the connection time

writing threatening letters

, but this matter was initiated by A Gui, who was on the run, and Chen Genlin, a local, provided information. After investigation, the police found that Chen Genlin was Ma Bosun's chauffeur. Ma had a private car with the number 1640.) arrested accomplices

Zhang Gengsheng, a local (totaling five people), at No. 2, Huaqing Lane, Fanghong Road, Nanshi. At around 8:00 AM, Wang Yiting and others were sent to the Criminal Court of Special District One. According to Ma Bosun's report, he was from Jiangwan, 24 years old, and lived at No. 902 Haiphong Road. Chen Genlin was his chauffeur, but as to whether Chen

was involved

in this case, he was not aware. However, Sun Xiaomao had visited Chen Genlin at his home once. He said that a Chen, namely Zhang Gengsheng, was related to the Ma family, but Ma did not pay him the money and had a quarrel with him. Therefore, he asked him to write a letter to demand it. However, the names at the end of the letter were all fabricated.

Chen Genlin

denied providing information. The other three defendants also denied involvement. Judge Tan Xinzhen reviewed the confession and ordered the defendants to be detained for further interrogation in seven days.

It is estimated that the stolen goods from the Weihaigwei Road case were 6 liang and 1 fen of gold, converted into 623.8 yuan. The gold ring from the Jing'an Villa case was converted into 16 yuan. Yesterday morning, Judge Chuan Lin summoned him to the Criminal Court Five for interrogation. Chuan Xingmao hired lawyer Jiang Yiping as his representative, who argued that the prices of the items received were not too low, and that according to Article 5 of the Association's Articles of Association, the police should only be notified if suspicious circumstances were discovered. Also, the loss report should be delivered within five days of the incident, but this time the loss report was received on the sixth day, so he could not be held responsible. The court stated that the case still required Chen Zhiliang to be brought to court, as well as the clerk who redeemed the stolen goods and the investigation of the delivery date of the loss report. It was announced that the hearing would be adjourned.

Robbery and Capture of Gang Leader in Shanzhen, Huzhou

Recently, they received a tip that the gang leaders in the case, Chen Shenghong, Ruan Hanqing (also known as Yi Zhen), Zhou Bingwu (also known as Cao Jiapin), and others, were hiding in the Yangshupu area of the Shanghai Public Concession to avoid capture. Xu, along with Detective Hu and detectives Wu Shaoqing, Lu Xiang, and Wang Zhanyuan, rushed to Shanghai overnight. Together with the police, at 7:00 AM on the fourth of this month, in heavy rain, they captured the three robbers one after another. They were sent to the First Special Court for interrogation. The report on the case of Chen and the three robbers being allowed to be transferred has already been published in this newspaper. Now, it is learned that Chen Shenghong, Ruan Hanqing, and Zhou Bingwu have been transferred to the First Brigade of the Zhejiang Provincial Water Police by the Fifth Team of Zhejiang yesterday for investigation. They will also strictly pursue and arrest the remaining gang members to ensure the peace and security of the area.
