Various Physical Evidence in the Case of the Japanese Sailor: Key Points of Identification Divided into Four Categories

Forensic Institute Reports Identification Results to Court

Shooting Distance Does Not Match Ye Haisheng's Demonstration

Fingerprint in Book Cannot Prove Yang Wendao

Traces in the Dug-out Room Were Not Caused by the Weight of the Pistol

No Human Cells or Tissues Found on the Bullet

This Case Will Be Continued This Afternoon

The case where Yang Wendao, Ye Haisheng, and Zhou Sherong, Cantonese, were accused by the Public Concession Bureau of killing Japanese sailor Nakayama Hideo on Doulean Road on November 9th of last year has been publicly tried by the First Special District Court's joint collegial panel several times. The court deemed it necessary to send the confiscated firearms, physics books, and recovered bullets for identification to the Zhenru Forensic Institute, so it announced a postponement of the trial. This has been reported in this newspaper many times. Now, the Forensic Institute has followed the court's instructions and conducted research on the case's pistol, bullets, Yang Wendao's fingerprints, and the books, based on the court's inquiries. The research has been completed, and a report has been made for each type of identification, totaling four identification reports. The reports detail the results obtained based on academic theory. These identification reports have been submitted to the First Special Court, so the court has scheduled a retrial for 2:00 PM today. The trial will still be conducted by a collegial panel, and the lawyer representing the police, Ru Baoyi, has recovered from his illness and will be replaced by Li Zhishan. Ru will appear in court today. The Special Court has instructed the police to summon the Korean Jack and the Japanese-Chinese doctor Zheng Huimin for questioning, but they have not appeared in court due to various reasons. The Public Concession Bureau is currently in contact with the Japanese Consulate, hoping that the two witnesses can testify in court today. Whether they can appear is still unknown. If time permits, the debate may begin, but it depends on the progress of the trial. It is difficult to predict at this time. Now, the points of identification requested by the First Special Court from the Forensic Institute and the results of the Institute's identification are excerpted below. The academic explorations in the identification report are omitted because the full text is four large volumes, totaling tens of thousands of words.

Shooting Distance

(1) The Special Court requested an investigation into whether the distance Ye Haisheng indicated when demonstrating the shooting at the scene of the incident, which was about five or six steps behind the victim Japanese sailor Nakayama Hideo, was consistent with the victim's injuries. Two photos of the victim's injuries and a diagram of the diagnosis certificate were included for rapid identification. The Institute made an identification and produced an identification report, which included eleven photos. The conclusion generally stated that the distance of the presumed shooting is usually based on the traces around the wound. Although the distance at the time of the shooting can also be inferred from the angle formed by the entry and exit points of the bullet, it can only be based on the normal state of the victim and shooter. If the head is tilted up or down, it cannot be speculated afterwards. According to the traces around the wound on the right side of the posterior mandible of Nakayama Hideo, the shooting distance is about five centimeters, which is inconsistent with Ye Haisheng's demonstration of five or six steps away from the victim, and it is not the condition that can be formed at about fifty centimeters as estimated in the diagnosis certificate. That is, according to the angle marked on the diagnosis certificate, if the perpetrator is estimated to have fired the pistol at a distance of five steps, that is, about three meters and forty centimeters from the victim, and after subtracting the length of the right arm, there are still about two meters and seventy centimeters left. If the shooter fired at a location of two meters and seventy centimeters while lying on the ground, it can still form the angle marked on the diagnosis certificate. Considering all the above points, according to the condition of the bullet entry point in the photo, it is definitely not a wound that can be formed by shooting from a distance of five steps behind the victim.

Fingerprint in Book

The First Special Court sent Yang Wendao's fingerprint on a single sheet of paper, requesting identification of whether it matches the fingerprint found in the book. According to the Institute's conclusion, the description of fingerprints is extremely complex, so the fingerprints left on the evidence can be used as the basis for criminal investigation. Although there are several incomplete fingerprints left in the physics book sent earlier, they are all incomplete short lines, and the monthly lines are not clear. On the lower part of page 37 of the book, there is a light blue incomplete fingerprint, the color of which is similar to the color of the edge of the hole dug in the book, and it seems that the central and left or right triangular patterns are missing. Only a few short lines are left, and detailed research has been conducted within the possible range of the remaining lines. The fingerprints of the left and right hands of Yang Wendao, which were sent for comparison, were also compared with each other. Because the light blue fingerprint left at the bottom of page 37 of the book is only a rectangular pattern of a part of the finger, and there is no special feature that can be seen, it cannot be proved that there are also such lines in Yang Wendao's fingerprints.

Hole in the Book

(3) The First Special Court sent pistol No. 241146 and a practical physics book, requesting identification of how long it would take for rust to appear if the pistol were hidden in the hole dug in the book, whether the traces and horizontal pressure marks in the book were left naturally or artificially, whether there were blue pencil marks at the binding of the book (i.e., the right page of page 16), how long the blue color has been left on the paper, whether the knife marks around the hole dug in the book are old or new, and how long has passed since the hole was dug. The Institute made various studies in the identification report and attached nine photos. The conclusion was that it would take some time for rust to appear if the pistol were hidden in the hole dug in the book. Rust is the oxidation of iron in the air to form iron oxide, which is yellowish-red-brown, and is called rust. The temperature of the air in the place where it is placed and whether there is grease attached to the surface of the pistol can affect the speed of chlorination. Therefore, only rust cannot estimate the time it has been collected. Whether the traces and horizontal pressure marks in the book were left naturally or artificially. After detailed comparison, the distance or length of each line of the horizontal pressure marks in the book examined earlier is consistent with the straight raised lines on the back of the barrel. Therefore, this pistol or a pistol of the same brand and size can leave such pressure marks. However, the pressure marks are deep, and there are two holes formed on the paper opposite the pistol's safety. The one in front is the imprint of the safety mechanism when it is closed, and the one in the back is the imprint when the safety is opened. The edges are turned up with rust spots and oil stains. The pressure marks in front are as deep as ten pages, and when irradiated with ultraviolet light, they show obvious oil stain fluorescence, which should be oil stains. The horizontal traces are located above, from page 16 to page 12, and are very clear. The ones located below, from page 1283 to page 399, are also very clear. The weight of the pistol is only 600 grams, and it is not easy to form such deep traces and holes even if it is placed in the book for a long time. Therefore, such deep penetrating pressure marks are not easy to form without external pressure. For example, heavy books or other heavy objects may have fallen on the book, and the pistol-shaped hole dug in the book is about 0.6 centimeters longer than the pistol, so the pistol can still move in the hole. If there is shaking, it may form this kind of hole. If only relying on the weight of the pistol itself, it seems that it cannot be arranged to form the existing falling traces in the book. The blue pencil marks are left at the binding of the book (i.e., the right page of page 16). The blue color has been left on the paper for some time. The blue writing is drawn with a blue pencil containing wax. The color of this kind of trace is not easy to change. Therefore, there is a lack of proper methods to explain the length of time after the drawing. The hole dug in the book was dug with a knife. Whether the knife marks around the dug hole are old or new, and how long has passed since the hole was dug. The gun-shaped marks in the book are neat around, and only slightly rough on the left side. The color is not significantly different from the color of the paper surface. In general paper cut marks, the age can be judged by the depth of the color, but the gun-shaped cut marks inspected this time are in the book, and it is not easy to contact with external light and dust, so it is difficult to measure the time elapsed.

Bullet Bloodstains

(4) The First Special Court sent a No. 19 bullet, requesting identification of whether it had passed through the human body, whether there were bloodstains, whether bloodstains could not be left if the bullet passed through the human body, and whether they could be detected after wiping off the bloodstains. The Institute attached two photos and concluded that no bloodstains were found on the bullets sent for inspection, and no human tissue cells were found in the precipitate of the bullet immersion solution. Can bloodstains not be left if the bullet passes through the human body? If it only penetrates a part of the human body and remains in the body, the bullet taken out by autopsy should have bloodstains and adherent human tissue cells. As for whether bloodstains should be left on the bullet if it passes through the human body and falls to other places, there is a lack of such literature and examples in forensic medicine for reference. However, according to theory, if a bullet passes through the human body, it should have attached human tissue. However, it is worth studying whether this situation differs due to the shooting distance. It is also worth studying whether the bloodstains attached to it can be destroyed by heat if the bullet penetrates the human body at that time, and how much the heat is reduced during the process of the bullet passing through the human body, and how the temperature reduction is recorded after passing through the air at different temperatures. There is also a lack of such literature in forensic medicine. The research on whether the human tissue attached to the bullet can be destroyed by heat involves the scope of ballistics, and this Institute lacks this equipment and cannot conduct experiments. It is only explained by the results of shooting animal experiments. Now, the chest and abdomen of live dogs are shot at distances of about 30 cm, 50 cm, and 1 meter with the same type of pistol and bullets. The bullets penetrate the body cavity and窜 into the cotton. Then, the bullets are taken out one by one, and detailed bloodstain examination and tissue cell examination are carried out by various methods. The results are all negative, and there are no bloodstains on the cotton attached to the bullets. According to the results of this kind of experiment, it can be known that bullets that penetrate the animal body in close-range shooting may not leave bloodstains. If there are bloodstains, if only wiped with paper or cloth, there will be bloodstains in the rifling and at the rear end of the bullet. If it has been treated with chemicals, it is to destroy human protein or soak in water for a long time, which can also cause the protein to dissolve and fall off. If there are the above-mentioned situations, it is impossible to detect human protein during the test. The above are all fair explanations based on academic facts. What needs to be explained is that this identification report was sent to the court, and the court notified the defense lawyers of the three defendants to come to the court to read it. Now it has been completed, so there may be fierce debates on this identification when the trial opens today.

Prosecutor Wang Ren examined the body and determined that he had died of illness. He ordered the Tongren Fuyuan Hall to prepare the body for burial, pending identification by relatives.

Central Bank Inspection Report

The 290th Inspection Report on the Issuance Reserve of Central Bank Exchange Notes states: "In accordance with the provisions of Article 13 of the Central Bank Law, this committee is responsible for inspecting the number of exchange notes issued by this bank and the reserve fund. The 290th inspection was held at the Issuance Bureau of this bank on July 4, 1936. The results of the inspection are reported as follows: (A) The total amount of exchange notes issued is 30,471,5506 yuan in silver dollars, including 27,348,7430 yuan in silver dollar notes and 3,122,8076 yuan in subsidiary currency notes. The total amount of exchange note reserve is 30,471,5506 yuan in silver dollars, including 20,654,4206 yuan in cash reserve. This cash reserve is held in the issuance headquarters and branches of this bank and various branches, totaling 10,280,0154.018 yuan, and 10,374,2665.82 yuan is deposited with other banks. The guaranteed reserve is equivalent to 98,171,300 yuan in silver dollars. (B) The total amount of customs gold exchange notes issued is 400,963.07 yuan. The total amount of the customs gold exchange special reserve fund is 400,963.07 yuan. This reserve fund includes 7,926.290 ounces of pure gold, valued at 51.68, equivalent to 400,963.07 yuan in customs gold. According to Article 22 of the Central Bank Law, the cash reserve shall be at least 60%, and the remainder shall be a guaranteed reserve consisting of legal collateral. The results of this inspection show that the cash reserve exceeds 60%, and the guaranteed reserve is within 40%, which is in compliance with the law. This report is hereby submitted. July 6, 1936, Chairman of the Board of Supervisors of the Central Bank, Li Fu-sun, Supervisors Xie Meng-jun, Bei Song-sun, Qin Run-qing, Yu Qia-qing, Lin Kang-hou, Xu Ji-qing."

Sales of Tiger Balm Ba Gua Dan Increase Sharply

Tiger Balm Ba Gua Dan, issued by Tiger Balm Yong An Tang, has been popular for a long time. Career Prospects for Graduates of the Nanyang Wireless Radio School

The Nanyang Wireless Radio Training School on Beile Road was founded by Liu Ping-shu, a wireless radio expert. Mr. Liu was the earliest and most vigorous advocate of vocational education in wireless radio in China. Therefore, the school's achievements are unmatched. Its equipment has been systematically added to over the past seven years, and its rich collection is rarely seen in private schools. Starting from the previous term, automatic machines were used to train telegraph transmission and reception skills, and student progress was even faster. As for the career prospects of the school's graduates, earlier graduates have spread throughout the provinces and cities. More than 100 are serving in this city. Students from the previous term have been hired by the Ministry of Communications Radio Station, the Jiangsu Provincial Construction Department Broadcasting Station, and the Central Bank Radio Station. The current students are about to graduate, and various telecommunications agencies are competing to hire them, with special representatives sent to test and recruit them. In view of the urgent needs of the outside world, the school has decided to greatly increase enrollment starting from the next term and will begin accepting new student registrations immediately.

The Tin Ingot Industry in Shanghai

— Chief Editor of China Credit Information

(Summary of Shanghai Industry and Commerce - 31)

1. Overview

The business nature of the tin ingot industry in this port is to smelt and melt tin ingots and sell them to general tin foil shops and tinware shops. However, there are slight differences between the past and the present. Five or six years ago, due to the light taxation on imported foreign tin, the tin shops in this port mainly sold tin ingots (commonly known as Dutch tin) from Singapore and the South Pacific islands. Later, due to the increase in import tariffs on foreign tin, there was no longer a substantial profit from importing it. As a result, domestic tin from Yunnan and Hunan provinces began to replace it. However, this domestic tin was unmelted. Therefore, the main business of tin shops in this port, in addition to the original transport of foreign tin, also needed to include the melting of domestic tin.

Of the tin ingots sold by tin shops in this port, 70% to 80% are used to make tin foil, and the remainder is used to make utensils and solder. Tin foil is as thin as paper, so the quality of the tin ingots required must be extremely pure. Those who make utensils can use slightly lower-grade tin (containing only 60% pure tin), while solder can be made with varying levels of purity. Imported Dutch tin has excellent quality, containing 99% pure tin, so it is exclusively used to make tin foil. However, it is almost entirely replaced by domestic tin nowadays. Domestic tin is named differently depending on the color after smelting, and its uses also vary. Now, they are listed as follows:

Fu Zu is the best of tin ingots, with a color grade between 99.7 and 8. Currently, it is rarely seen due to the high selling price.

Xiao Hong, also known as Gua Hong tin, is the most common tin ingot on the market, with a color grade of 99.34. Each ingot weighs 75 jin on the Sima scale.

Tong Guang: This tin ingot has an even lower color grade, containing only 50% to 60% pure tin. The remainder is aluminum and impurities, which are made by melting old tinware and tin foil ash.

Gou Guang: Its color is slightly inferior to Bi Guang, but it is still used to make tinware.

Solder: The color varies, but it is also the worst.

In addition, the tin sold on the market also varies in name depending on its source. Now, the main ones are listed below:

Gejiu Tin is named after Gejiu County in Yunnan Province. It has the largest output among domestic products. However, the quality of Gejiu tin itself is inconsistent. The highest common color grade is 99.9, and the lowest is 84.5. Each ingot weighs more than 50 jin on the Sima scale.

Heng Tin is commonly known as Heng Dian and is produced in Hengzhou, Hunan Province. Its color grade ranges from 99.3 to 99.6. Each ingot is rectangular and weighs more than 50 jin on the Sima scale.

Jianghua Tin is produced in Jianghua, Hunan Province. Its color is excellent, at 99.9. It is also rectangular, and each ingot weighs 22-23 jin on the Sima scale.

Linwu Tin is produced in Linwu, Hunan Province. The color is the same as Jianghua tin. Each ingot weighs more than 50 jin on the Sima scale.

Ganzhou Tin is produced in Linwu, Jiangxi Province, with a color grade of around 99. When the ore tin is poured, it is placed in a wok, so it is shaped like a wok. Each ingot weighs more than 50 jin on the Sima scale. (To be continued)

Summer Vacation Student National Products Movement

— Yang An

Recently, the National Products community and the Education community have joined hands to organize this most valuable undertaking, namely, using students' summer vacations to engage in the National Products Movement, working hard to promote national products, and saving this unprecedented economic national crisis. At the reception for school principals the other day, it was increasingly recognized as a fundamental national salvation effort, and all were willing to do their best to carry it out in earnest. Principal Zheng Tong-he of Shangzhong School, Principal Jia Fo-ru of Zhonghua Vocational School, and Secretary Zhu You-huan of Guanghua University all said that promoting national products is the natural duty of citizens. After returning to school, we will immediately guide students' work and send a circular to students who have returned to their hometowns to do the same. After the start of school, we will also hold a student national products movement achievement exhibition to display the activities of the students during the vacation. Mr. Zheng also contributed two points: Those in leadership positions must first lead by example, use national products, and extend this to relatives and friends, which will surely have a significant effect. It is best to devote more effort to promoting national products in the mainland so that the people in the mainland have the ability to recognize national products. Mr. Huang Ren-zhi said: "Promoting national products is not only for the development of national product manufacturers themselves but also for the entire national product industry and the entire country. Recently, the problem of smuggling has become increasingly serious, and the entire national product industry is on the verge of collapse, and the results are unbearable. In this extraordinary period, all sectors of society must rise up to promote national products and fight for this last chance. I have previously dedicated myself to the education community, and now I am willing to devote my remaining strength to serve the national product community," and so on. The enthusiasm of this energetic Mr. Huang moved everyone present. And the practical actions of the educational leaders, Zheng and Jia, in advocating for students are indeed rare. This summer vacation student national products movement is in line with President Chiang's advocacy of students serving society. I hope that our student community will use this year's summer vacation for this national product movement to save the country and society. Through investigation, persuasion, lectures, organization, exhibitions, research, and reports, we will all work hard for the country with our own blood. If the entire student community can be mobilized to carry out this national product movement to save the country, its great influence and effectiveness will be immeasurable. I know that with enthusiastic and striving principals, there will inevitably be enthusiastic and striving students. With a tireless spirit, we will continue to work, shedding light on the situation and eliminating smuggling. The fate of our national product industry may have a turning point and hope. After this grand meeting, I offer my sincere admiration and wish the success of this year's student national products movement.

The National Products Movement Needs Three Types of Assistance

— Cun

The National Products Movement, on the surface, seems to have reached a considerably successful stage. Large factories and large-scale national products companies are springing up one after another, but when we examine the reality, we still feel that it is in its infancy. For example, various important machines must rely on foreign supply, and some raw materials (such as the finest spun yarn, rayon, etc.) are mostly purchased from overseas. The management system of industry and commerce is also a forced imitation of foreign models. Whether it can adapt to the environment and needs of our National Products Movement is still a question worthy of discussion.

The National Products Movement should be practical and suited to the needs of the nation. It should not focus solely on Westernization, as this may hinder the progress of the National Products Movement. So, what are the types of assistance needed for the National Products Movement?

Scientific Assistance: The 20th century is an era of science. A country without science will inevitably decline and even lead to national subjugation. Look at our China, where science is equal to zero. Large-scale undertakings such as electrical engineering, chemical engineering, and machinery manufacturing all rely on foreign countries. Therefore, the National Products Movement must first cultivate great scientists to invent and create all machines, chemical engineering, and other large-scale engineering projects. In this way, the National Products Movement can succeed, and the Republic of China can have a national products nation.

Government Assistance: In addition to cultivating and encouraging scientists, the government should also assist and build large industries. It should make an overall plan for the country, how to resist foreign goods, how to make the National Products Movement successful, create a completely national products nation, and how to be able to promote national products abroad... These are all the responsibilities of the government.

Public Assistance: Now we are being oppressed by imperialism to the point of suffocation, and yet some of the people still promote foreign goods and disregard national products. This is a path to self-destruction. Therefore, the public should wake up, and everyone should not buy foreign goods but completely use national products, so that the national products made by the Chinese people can be enjoyed by the Chinese people themselves.

The above three are related and cannot be separated and carried out independently. The three must advance simultaneously in unity.

National Products Salesman

— Yiyi Guan Zhu

We often hear people refer to those who welcome "foreign goods," the "foreign fanatics," as "foreign goods salesmen." As the name suggests, it naturally means that he or she purchases "foreign goods" for everything in daily life: eating, wearing, and using, which is tantamount to helping "foreign goods" shops promote business! How shameful and embarrassing is this?

You must know that a decent Chinese person should use their own good "national products" when they already have them. If they have good "national products" but do not use them and insist on using "foreign goods," this is "self-abandonment"! Self-abandonment is despised by mankind, and even the foreigners who sell you the goods and earn your money cannot help but secretly ridicule you for "not loving your country." Think about it, isn't this embarrassing and the most shameful thing?

Ah! Friends! Now we won't talk nonsense anymore. In short, I hope you will examine yourselves and ask yourselves honestly whether you are a "foreign goods salesman"? If not, then of course you are worthy of our respect, and at the same time, I hope you will work even harder. If you are, then we sincerely advise you to wake up and, from now on, for all daily necessities, as well as those related to eating and wearing, purchase "national products." In other words, we want to advise you to become a "national products salesman." That is glorious! That has face!

Inserting Tobacco Stems to Resist Rice Borers

— Sun Lin-chang

My China is known as an agricultural country, and grain is its main product, listed as one of the export commodities. However, in recent years, the facts have shown that the opposite is true. Although this is due to local instability and successive droughts and floods, it is also caused by rice borer infestation. According to expert estimates, the losses caused by rice borers to my country's rice crops amount to tens of millions of yuan annually. The harm of floods does not reach the highlands, and the drought does not reach the lowlands. However, the severity of rice borer infestation makes it possible for the plague to spread to farmland regardless of height.

"Inserting tobacco stems to resist rice borers" has been repeatedly tested and proven effective by the Zhejiang Provincial Entomology Bureau. At the same time, it can promote rice growth and increase production. The method of application is to insert the tobacco stems next to the rice branches about four weeks after transplanting the rice seedlings, one stem per clump. It is even better if two or three replacements can be made before the rice ears emerge. This method is inexpensive, effective, and easy to implement. Now that the season for planting rice seedlings has arrived, farmers in various affected areas may wish to try it and observe the results. Moreover, in recent years, various provinces in my country have produced tobacco leaves. Since tobacco stems can prevent and control rice borers, if they can be widely used throughout the country in the future, it will also be a way to utilize waste and maintain the rural economy.

My Country's Football Team's European Tour

Written and sent by Team Captain Li Huitang

According to my observations in Medan football, when I first arrived in this land in the early 1920s, their level was quite mediocre. Many players were not good at using their heads. Their immaturity was on par with the Saigon teams at the time. Whenever there was a match, we knew we would win and were never cautious. Unexpectedly, in the past six years, through contact and observation with foreign teams, their skills have improved rapidly, by leaps and bounds. As the saying goes, "A scholar who has been away three days must be looked at with new eyes." Their level has greatly improved, making foreign teams dare not underestimate them. In particular, the progress of Malaysian players is most remarkable. Last year, Nanhua, with an incomplete team, was severely defeated by them. When the news arrived, I initially couldn't believe it. Today, witnessing it firsthand, I know they are indeed extraordinary. Their victory over Nanhua was not a fluke. On the other hand, our country is stuck in its ways, with slow progress in recent years, or even no progress at all. The Medan football team, which we thought was not worth mentioning six years ago, has now followed and caught up, and even has a tendency to overtake us. I think if this continues, they will advance a step, and we will retreat a foot. The future of our country's football is not optimistic. It is most beneficial to invite strong foreign teams to China for matches. I hope the authorities can shoulder this difficult task and realize this hope and work.

Penang Island

After our team defeated all the teams in Medan, we bought a boat at 5 PM on June 17 and set off for Penang Island. Penang Island is a small island in northern Malaysia, about the same size as Hong Kong, facing Medan across a narrow strip of water. The fourteen-hour voyage was not painful. We arrived at the port early in the morning on the 18th. Consul Huang, representatives of overseas Chinese organizations, reporters, and many others came to welcome us, crowding the dock with no space left. We took cars to the Shanghai Hotel to rest. After lunch, we took several cars to the small port of "George Town," fifty miles from Penang Island, to prepare for the afternoon match with the town's selected team. After arriving at the port, we were welcomed by various groups holding meetings. The ceremony was the same as in other places. Director Rong and the reporter expressed their gratitude. At around 5 PM, the following players put on their uniforms and met with the selected team:

Bao Jiaping, Cai Wenli, Mai Shaohan, Liang Shutang, Liang Rongzhao, Zhang Xianyuan, Zheng Jiliang, Tan Jiangbai, Sun Jinshun, Huang Meishun, Yang Shuiyi

The score was 5-0 in the first half and 8-1 at the end. Jiangbai scored twice, Shuiyi scored two, Meishun and Jinshun scored one each. Acting Captain Bao Jiaping. George Town is a small town with a sparse population. The Nanhua team came here once years ago. Although today is unprecedentedly lively, there are less than 3,000 spectators in the entire stadium. The level of football here is also relatively immature. Our team's lineup was not very strong, but it was more than enough. The entire match became our team's world, and the battle was not tense at all. Jiangbai's head and foot kicks, scoring four goals alone, were most praised by the audience. There is nothing else worth mentioning. In the evening, we were treated to a feast. After dinner, we drove back to Penang, arriving at our residence at 11 PM.

(June 19) Today, our team is scheduled to play against the Penang United team. This morning, all the overseas Chinese organizations on the island held a welcome meeting and a flag-presenting ceremony. Consul Huang and representatives from business, academic, and other circles delivered speeches. Director Rong and I were invited to speak successively. After the photo session and tea party, everyone dispersed. The match started at 5 PM. Our team played with the following lineup on the left wing and the result was a 0-0 draw:

Bao Jiaping, Tan Jiangbai, Li Tiansheng, Chen Zhenhe, Xu Yahui, Liang Rongzhao, Zheng Jiliang, Zhuo Shijin, Li Huitang, Sun Jinshun, Cao Guicheng

Penang Island's football strength occupies a considerable position in Malaysia. However, the local people, seeing our team's excellent performance in Singapore, believed that the island was no match for us, and some even bet that our team would win by more than four goals. Who knew that things in the world are always unexpected? After a fierce battle, both sides gained nothing, and the match ended in a draw. The reason why their team was able to avoid defeat was half due to the effective defense and half due to luck. Our shots were often decisive, but many hit the goalposts or crossbars and bounced back, failing to break through the goal. The opponent's defense was strict and effective. The central defender stubbornly defended his home, refusing to cross the midline even a step. In addition, our front-line performance was mediocre, and although we launched many attacks, we failed to succeed. In the second half, our side was in danger several times, but fortunately, the defenders were still good, preventing any negligence. Since Feng and Ye, two forwards, were injured in Medan, Jinshun is too fat, Shijin is weak, and Xianyuan is not a forward material, we feel the lack of a sharp blade. If Feng and Ye do not recover soon, there will be many strong enemies in the future, which is a cause for concern for our team's attacking power. After the match, the Penang Football Association welcomed us with refreshments. Director Rong responded in English. After returning to our residence, we packed our luggage and prepared to go to Yangon tomorrow.

Central Subsidies for Education Funds in Various Provinces and Regions in the 25th Year

The Municipal Education Bureau Strictly Rectifies Private Schools

The Anglo-French College is Deemed to Have Falsely Claimed Approval and is Shut Down

The Donghai Commercial Vocational School is Ordered to Correct Its Misleading Recruitment Advertising

The Cihang Vocational School is Ordered to Stop Recruiting Students for Not Obtaining Approval

The Municipal Education Bureau's supervision and guidance of private schools has always been extremely strict. Inspectors are dispatched at any time to investigate and order improvements or shut them down. As schools are busy recruiting students during the summer vacation, some unscrupulous schools falsely claim to be approved and advertise in newspapers. Fearing that young students may be deceived and affect their future, inspections are even stricter. The Education Bureau has shut down the Anglo-French College and other schools. Details are as follows:

Anglo-French College Falsely Claims Approval

The Anglo-French College at 470 Old Baz Road, which was established by a Mr. Lambarde, who claims to be a student of Oxford University, has recently been publishing advertisements in various newspapers. In addition to using the name "College" without authorization, it also falsely claims to have been approved by the Municipal Education Bureau. The Education Bureau has discovered this and has sent a letter to the Public Works Department to shut it down, in order to prevent members of the public from being deceived.

Donghai Commercial Vocational School Misuses Its Name

The Donghai Junior Commercial Vocational School on Liaoyang Road, Hongkou District, has recently been recruiting students in newspapers under the name "Donghai Middle School." The Municipal Education Bureau believes that this is very inappropriate and has ordered the school to correct it immediately and not to recruit students under the name of a middle school, otherwise it will be shut down.

Cihang Vocational School Stops Recruiting

The Cihang Vocational School on Hart Road, Connaught Road, which was only recently established, has been ordered by the Municipal Education Bureau to stop recruiting students because it has not obtained approval to operate. It has also notified newspapers to stop publishing the school's recruitment advertisements.

China Health Education Society Exhibition

Preparations are Intense

The opening date of the Health Education Exhibition organized by the China Health Education Society's first annual meeting is approaching, and the work is very intense. Work is also carried out normally on Sundays. It is reported that there are more than 90 participating groups in the first, second, third, and fourth exhibition halls, with a total of more than 10,000 exhibits. In addition to being held at the Zhenjiang People's Education Museum in Jiangsu Province, a fifth exhibition hall is specially set up for health education supplies, which will be displayed at the Provincial Medical and Political College. The hall has now been renovated, with a total of seven major areas and 32 units. Exhibitors include New Asia Pharmaceutical Factory, Wuzhou Factory, Sino-French Pharmaceutical Factory, Xinyi Pharmaceutical Factory, Sino-Western Pharmaceutical Factory, Minsheng Pharmaceutical Factory, Tiger Balm Yong An Tang Bayer Pharmaceutical Company, Commercial Press, China Bookstore, World Bookstore, Zhengzhong Medical Bureau, Kaiming Bookstore, Datong Book Style, A & F Swiss Condensed Milk Company, and more than 20 other companies. Yesterday, various factories and bureaus sent exhibit staff to arrange the exhibition. The association also set up a temporary liaison office at the Zhenjiang West Gate Station. This exhibition has a national character and welcomes schools and groups to attend and participate.

(Nanjing, 7th Dispatch) According to the report of Jiang Zhaoju's inspection of obstetrics schools in Hubei, Hunan, and Henan provinces, the Ministry of Education specially issued orders to the education departments of the three provinces in July, instructing them to forward the instructions on the points that should be improved in each province for compliance.

(Chengdu, 6th Dispatch) The fifth joint graduation examination for secondary schools in Sichuan Province was held in various districts this morning. In the Chengdu district, 1,168 students took the examination. It is scheduled to finish on the 8th and the results will be announced in a week.

Holds Board Meeting

The Sino-German Cultural Association held its third board meeting in Beijing on the 6th. Zhu Jiajia presided over the meeting. The agenda included: (1) Passing the motion to appoint Elgnar Krahayn as an honorary member; (2) Passing the motion to select domestic students to study in Germany; (3) Guangzhou Hair Dou proposed to organize a liaison office of the Association in Guangdong. Lü Jiong Serves as Acting Director of the Institute of Meteorology of the Academia Sinica

Zhu Kezhen, President of Zhejiang University, was originally the Director of the Institute of Meteorology of the Academia Sinica. However, due to the University Organization Law, which stipulates that the President cannot hold other positions concurrently, President Cai has granted him a year's leave from the position of Director and appointed Lü Jiong as the acting director.

Sichuan University Runs Training Courses

The education departments of Sichuan and Guizhou provinces, following the instructions of the Ministry of Education, decided to run a summer training course for secondary school teachers and staff at Sichuan University during the summer vacation. Classes are scheduled to officially begin on the 25th, with a training period of one month. The quota is currently set at 320, of which 240 are assigned and 80 are free to participate. The training subjects are divided into four types: English, Mathematics, Physics and Chemistry, and History and Geography. The operating expenses are being requested by the education department to be allocated by Liu Xiang.

Strictly Implementing the System of Full-Time Teachers

The Jiangsu Education Department Orders All Schools

The Jiangsu Provincial Education Department issued an order to the principals of all provincial secondary schools, saying, "According to the request of teachers' representatives of provincial secondary schools Zhang Tongmo, Wu Zonghan, Rong Weisheng, etc., issue an order to all principals to strictly allocate salaries in accordance with the salary standards for full-time teachers and not to calculate them according to hours, etc. In this regard, this department previously promulgated the salary standards for teachers in provincial secondary schools, the purpose of which is to concentrate tasks and improve treatment. For the past three years, most schools have been able to conscientiously follow this, but there are also many schools that superficially comply but still calculate salaries according to hours, which is contrary to the original intention of this department to implement the full-time teacher system. In view of the previous situation, in addition to issuing separate orders, this order is hereby issued to inform the principal of the school that in the future, when hiring teachers, they must strictly comply with the regulations. This order."

Guangdong Province Holds Examinations for Municipal Elementary School Principals

(Hong Kong, 7th Dispatch) Registration for the Guangdong Provincial Municipal Elementary School Principal Examination will close on the 8th. The Examination Committee will review the qualifications and the examination period is scheduled for the 15th at the Municipal Government.

Opening Ceremony on the 12th in Zhenjiang

Chu Minyi Discusses the Sino-French Institute of Technology

Yesterday, Central Committee Member Chu Minyi arrived in Shanghai. A reporter from the Central News Agency visited the Sino-French National Institute of Technology. When asked about the recent situation of the school, he gave a very detailed explanation, which is recorded as follows:

We have been devoted to Sino-French educational and cultural undertakings for many years. Our purpose is to cultivate outstanding young people in our country to become useful talents. The method is to transport the spiritual and material civilization of France to China, and at the same time spread our culture to France, so that the educational and cultural undertakings of these two great countries can be integrated and advanced together. It is because the relationship between China and France is very close, and both countries are republics, and the national characters of the two countries are also very similar. Therefore, the joint development of educational and cultural undertakings is more cordial and convenient than with other countries. Efforts in this regard that have already achieved results include the Franco-Chinese Labor and Diligence Society, presided over by Wu Zhihui and Li Shizeng, and the Sino-French University in Lyon, which have cultivated a large number of talents. The outstanding people among them are scattered in all directions, serving the country and society, and are able to make achievements. Among the educational institutions in China, there is the Sino-French University in Beiping, founded by Mr. Li Shizeng. The only one jointly run by the governments of China and France is our school. Our school was established in the tenth year of the Republic of China. Before that, it was Tongji University, run by Germans. Because of the European War, according to the Treaty of Versailles, all the school property was transferred to the governments of China and France. Therefore, the scale and equipment of our school, all the buildings, machinery and instruments, were mostly left by the Germans, and have already been established. In addition, the machinery and instruments made in France have been managed and operated, and the work has been increasingly effective. Initially, there were two departments of industry and commerce, but now it has been changed to an independent college of engineering. Our college is divided into two departments: university and high school. The university department has four grades, and the high school has three grades. There is also a one-year French language preparatory class, progressing step by step. To graduate, students must undergo eight years of cultivation. By the time they reach the third year of university, they are divided into two departments: civil engineering, railway engineering, mechanical engineering, and electrical engineering, so that each can learn according to their interests. Therefore, after graduation, students have gained in-depth knowledge and become industrial specialists who can be self-reliant. Those who rank first in the examination results will be funded by our college to study in France, Belgium, and other countries. In addition, university and high school students with excellent academic performance, who rank in the top four, will also be exempt from tuition fees as a reward. As for tuition fees, the middle school department only charges fifteen yuan per semester, and the university department only charges twenty-five yuan per semester. Accommodation is completely free. If students can be frugal, then a few hundred yuan a year is enough for food, books, and other expenses. Regarding studying abroad, we will pay special attention to it. In the past, we have funded a large number of students to study abroad. There have been two batches funded by our college expenses, each with twenty people. There have been seven people funded by the Sino-British Boxer Indemnity Committee. Last year, the Sino-French Education Fund Committee also funded two people to France. Since the 23rd year, the Sino-British Boxer Indemnity Committee has subsidized two people to Belgium every year. The previous forty-seven people have all graduated and returned to China, and each has a corresponding task. As for the graduates of previous sessions, those who are in China are also introduced to work by our college, and each gets what they want. This year's graduates include eight from the civil engineering and railway engineering department and six from the mechanical and electrical engineering department. The Department of Railways has organized an examination committee according to the regulations, with one member each from the Ministry of Railways, the Ministry of Industry, and the Construction Committee, and the French side has sent a committee to take the examination together, to show prudence. Previously, the middle school attached to our college was not part of the joint examination, because it belonged to the nature of a preparatory class for industrial specialties, and the curriculum was slightly different from ordinary high schools. This year, it will also follow the order of the Ministry to participate in the joint examination. As for the internal administration, special attention will be paid to moral education. The management of our college has always been very strict. Starting from the next semester, a military management system will be adopted to militarize school discipline. Regarding equipment, our college has been limited by funds in the past and has not been able to expand as much as possible. Now, with the donation from the Sino-British Boxer Indemnity Committee, we have purchased a large number of physical and chemical instruments and books from the Academia Sinica to enrich various teaching materials. In short, to the best of our ability, we will spare no effort to promote the bright future of our college and seek the common development of Sino-French educational and cultural undertakings. Recalling the past few decades, this ambition has never changed. In the future, we will continue to work hard based on the established policy and method. This is our duty and cannot be neglected.

Pure Gold Prices Fall, Standard Gold Margin Drops by Sixty Cents

Major Players Moderately Offloading Positions

The gold market yesterday saw a decline in pure gold prices, with major players moderately offloading their positions, gradually weakening the market from a stable start. However, buyers also maintained their presence by taking advantage of the lower prices, resulting in extreme stagnation after the initial decline. According to reports, the overseas silver market saw the British pound rise and the US dollar remain stable in the morning. Traders indicated that there was some Indian buying after the market closed, but the supply was limited, leading to stable market conditions. The forward silver price in Mont de Piété remained unchanged or rose by five haos. Exchange rates slightly increased, the London spot gold price fell by two pence, and the central bank's listed exchange rates for the British pound and the US dollar remained unchanged. The customs gold unit dropped by three li. The standard gold margin price was listed at 1,130 yuan, and the over-the-counter preliminary transaction opened at around 38 yuan. Hengyu Dadecheng's margin increased slightly. The market opened flat, and remained stable after opening. Major players offloaded their positions, gradually pushing prices down. HSBC's listed exchange rates for the British pound and the US dollar remained unchanged, and the silver equalization tax increased by 0.25. At this point, spot dealers made some purchases, leading to some struggle, but the overall trend was fatigue in the afternoon due to Dingkang's offloading. The market was extremely stagnant, with only two jiaos of fluctuation. The market was extremely dull, and the current margin was still 1.6 yuan lower than Sida. The day's market conditions are recorded below:

The market opened at 1,138.3 yuan, unchanged from the previous close. Dadecheng rose to 8.5 yuan. Dingkang, Jinfeng, Yongda, Dadecheng, Chunyuan, and Yong sold positions, falling back to 7.7 yuan. HSBC's listed exchange rates remained unchanged, and the silver equalization tax increased by 0.25. At this point, Hengyu, Futai, Tingfu, Yutongfeng, and Heng's margin rose to 7.9 yuan, struggling to maintain prices, while Dingkang's selling pressure was strong, pushing prices down to 7.7 yuan again. The market closed for the morning at 1,137.8 yuan.

The market opened in the afternoon at 1,137.8 yuan. Hengyu Huixiang sold down to 7.6 yuan. Xianghe and Qingfa Yong's margin rose to 1,137.7 yuan. There were no changes in between.

The closing price was the central bank's standard gold margin price, listed at 1,130 yuan. In terms of the closing price, it rose by less than eight yuan, and was four jiaos higher than the previous close. The registered price for this month was 1,134 yuan, and for August it was 1,138 yuan. The morning water supplement was 1,134 yuan, and the afternoon price was the same. The price of pure gold was 8 yuan higher, at 1,146.3 yuan. The spot market remained stable. Tianjin goods were 12.5 yuan higher, and cooked pure gold was 11.5 yuan higher, but there were few sellers. Cooked pure gold was 15.5 yuan higher. Shengyuan Yong sold 70 taels to jewelry stores. The current gold margin for the August contract was reduced by 1.6 yuan by Yuanmaoyong and delivered to Shengyuan Yong for 63 contracts.

Transactions in the market were scarce. In summary, Tongfengheng, Hengyu Huixiang, Yuanmaoyong, Fuyu, Hongkang, Yongqingfa, Yongxianghe, and others were on the buying side, while Dadecheng, Chunyuanyong, Dingkang, and Fuxingyong were on the selling side. Hengyu and Huixiang went in and out first.

In summary, the day's market was stable and fatigued. The market opened in the morning at 1,138.3 yuan, and closed in the afternoon at 1,137.7 yuan. The highest price was 1,138.5 yuan, and the lowest price was 1,137.6 yuan, with a fluctuation of nine jiaos. As a result, it fell by six jiaos compared to the previous close. There were 1,953 contracts remaining for this month, with 11 long positions and 9 short positions. Yarn and Cotton: Profit-Taking Longs Exit, Yarn Market Declines and Falls

The yarn market rose in the morning and fell in the afternoon, and the situation became more chaotic. The market sentiment was still firm, and the market speculators were unusually enthusiastic, so the waves were very large. In fact, the futures yarn has been rising sharply for several days, and the current sales of customers have not yet developed in large quantities, which is somewhat unsatisfactory. It is said that securities firms took profits in the afternoon, and British factories opened 3,000 bales of cotton yarn, which led to a decline and fall.

The Standard Yarn Slid Downstream Step by Step in the Afternoon

The standard yarn market opened in the morning, and because Chinese cotton continued to rise, the market was calm, and the months were uneven, up and down by two or three jiaos. The second board continued to weaken. Unexpectedly, at the third closing, Tongji and the bulls came to absorb again. It was rumored that the flour market had not yet opened for auction, and the atmosphere suddenly became tense, and the buying frenzy suddenly rose. Each month jumped up by 1.4 or 5 yuan. As a result, each month rose by 0.3, 7, 8, 9 jiaos to 1.1 yuan compared with the closing price of the previous day. The market opened in the afternoon, and the momentum gradually softened, and sellers were lacking. Each month fell by six, seven, or eight jiaos, but later tended to go downstream step by step. This is because the securities gang's bulls came out, and the platform became loose. However, Fengtai came out in the morning and went in in the afternoon. As a result, each month fell by 1.4, 6, or 8 jiaos compared with the morning closing price. First Month of New Cocoons: Silk Export Report

August 1st… Commencement of Raw Silk Quality Inspection

New Cocoons Next Year… Implementation of Raw Silk Grading Inspection

According to a report from the Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau of the Ministry of Industry, in June, silk exports totaled 2,459 bales of white filature silk, 268 bales of other silks, and 1,215 bales of waste silk, for a total of 3,942 bales. This is slightly less than the 4,798 bales in the same month last year. However, this month marks the beginning of the new cocoon season. During this month, silk merchants are actively purchasing spring cocoons and preparing factory sites, making them quite busy. Market transactions mostly involve discarding old stock and adopting new. Spot exports are necessarily fewer. According to a recent survey, after the arrival of the spring cocoons, silk factories that have started operations include over twenty in Wuxi, twenty-five in various parts of Zhejiang, and forty-two in Shanghai, totaling over eighty. The atmosphere is quite vibrant. Furthermore, since being ordered by the Ministry in March to prepare for raw silk quality inspection, the local Commodity Inspection Bureau has been ordering various new types of inspection machinery and instruments from home and abroad, recruiting and training technical personnel, and actively preparing. It was originally scheduled to be implemented on July 1st, but due to the time-consuming nature of machinery installation, approval has been obtained from the Ministry to officially implement it on August 1st. The Bureau also convened a conference of silk industry representatives from Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Sichuan, and Shandong on June 22nd to solicit opinions from all parties, in order to pool ideas and benefit from collective wisdom. The silk industry representatives present expressed their support for the government's handling of raw silk quality inspection, in order to save the silk industry. The conference also decided to implement raw silk grading inspection after the arrival of the new cocoons next year. This one-year preparation period is to allow government and businesses to study proper measures to ensure timely implementation, it is said.

Spring and Autumn

Tidbits

— (Shigandang)

Stones on high mountains often easily fall into deep valleys.

Flowers that bloom profusely are not far from withering.

The silkworm's self-imposed cocoon is very worthy of praise, because it "secludes itself to cultivate," preparing to create a new life—a moth.

Filming movies relies on expressions; the better the expressions, the more they demonstrate the actor's superb skills. However, this is not the case in how people conduct themselves in the world. It is best to have no expression. For example, when one is angry inside, one still talks and laughs as usual on the surface, or when one is happy inside, one still acts as if nothing is happening. In short, one should not let anyone see one's joys, angers, sorrows, or pleasures on one's face. Showing deep expressions over trivial matters is not suitable for modern society.

Deep in the Mountains and Lakes

— Lake Beggar

To appreciate the scenery of Qiantang, one must ascend to Five Clouds and reach the ends of Heaven's Gate to truly grasp the subtle charm of the mountains and lakes. The Six Bridges and Two Embankments only offer its clarity, while the Dragon Well and Lingyin Temple merely capture its serenity. To seek a combination of grandeur and elegance, depth and vastness, one must ascend through the clouds and mist to faintly discern it. Most tourists in Hangzhou merely skim the surface while boating or take a brief, shallow climb, already feeling satisfied. Who understands that the natural beauty lies beyond the lightly adorned West Lake? Starting from the riverbank, one walks leisurely along the Hangzhou-Fuyang Road, embracing the shimmering waves on the left and swallowing the misty shadows on the right. The wind's murmur is still, as if the tongue and nose are expanding and contracting with the universe. As the morning sun gradually unfolds, the splashing water sprouts dark purple scales, incomparably beautiful. The fishing boats and sails are waiting for the tide to rise, as serene as newly molted frogs. Passing the Nine Dragon Heads, one reaches Fancun, where silk willows brush against one's chest, their green eyes gleaming. The village was once the place where Grand Master Lianchi resided. The homes in the small market are serene and elegant. Heading west, one traverses slopes and fields, entering the foothills, where dense shade blocks the sunlight. Though the sun's rays may be directly overhead outside the mountain, here, startled birds are just now chirping once or twice. Further ahead lies the Cloud Dwelling Bamboo Path, where tens of thousands of jade-green bamboos rub against each other on both sides, making a clear, ringing sound. Bamboo powder like snow covers the ground, making one's footsteps crystalline. Many of the bamboo tips have inscriptions, proclaiming someone's act of releasing captive animals, showing the devoutness of these men and women. It is laughable. Following the left path, one ascends along the cliff, which is Five Clouds. Initially, the stone steps are smooth and even, but after three hundred steps, one gradually falters. One rests and climbs, looking down into bottomless space. All one sees is the midday smoke of ancient temples, thinly rising above the pine trees. The wind rolls it, often combining two, three, or even dozens of wisps at the top, while those extending from the gaps in the trees continue to rise, never ceasing. This scene is difficult to describe. On the mountain ridge is a pavilion called Lin Hai, from which one can overlook the Qiantang River. The rising water vapor only reveals a faint outline. Climbing further, the path becomes narrow and without steps, with wild vines helping one's hands and feet, yet one still fears exhaustion. After catching one's breath and sweating for about half an hour, one finally reaches Xingji Temple. The temple sits atop the mountain, open and unobstructed on all sides, with only one old tree in front of the gate, making the sound of raging waves on its own. The Buddhist fire is dim and cold, and the monk is lean and refined. Talking with him about the temple's history, the conversation transcends the Six Dynasties. Circling the Five Clouds Pavilion, one ascends even more desolate hills, pushing through grass and stepping carefully, not following the woodcutter's path. Passing Tea Leaf Mountain and Myriad Years Ridge, besides the sounds of wind and trees, one also hears the rhythmic songs of tea-picking girls, expressing their affection and not avoiding sensual themes, like a scene from ancient times. Descending Langdang Ridge, ten miles of lush greenery, one feels birds at one's armpits, suddenly understanding the story of Liezi riding the wind. At the end of the ridge, one touches the Lion Peak, which is not as high as Five Clouds, but more precipitous. At its summit, a stone stands upright, impossible for ordinary people to climb. Looking at Heaven's Gate, it still stands tall in the clouds. One walks with one's arms, fearing to fall in the wind. The chaotic peaks below are colored yellow and purple, vying for beauty, as the setting sun at one's feet conjures afterglows. Reaching Hugong Ridge, clouds seal the peaks, woodcutters and gatherers are nowhere to be seen. One hurries through the empty valley, startling birds with one's steps. Helpless, one seeks lodging at the Dragon Well Temple. All night, the sound of the stream answers the chime of bells and musical stones. One wonders if one has already entered another life.

Plain Boiled Water

— Zhu Ying

Hygienists don't drink tea or coffee; they only quench their thirst with plain boiled water. It is said that tea and coffee stimulate the nerves, while only by drinking plain boiled water can one quote classics and expound great principles, winning people's nods of approval and applause.

To people accustomed to drinking tea and coffee, plain boiled water always feels bland and tasteless, lacking the appeal of tea and coffee. However, a friend of mine who is used to drinking plain boiled water says, "Plain boiled water is like a simple country girl who doesn't understand worldly affairs. Naturally, she doesn't know anything about applying rouge and wearing high heels, nor does she know that there is such a thing as 'love' between men and women. But only such a naive and unpretentious woman is worthy of love. Loving women in pleasure quarters may seem intoxicating, but those who can intoxicate you can also cause you extreme sorrow, because the love of such women is mixed with ulterior motives, just as tea and coffee are not the original flavor. To seek the original flavor, one must experience it in plain boiled water."

Although this friend's theory is somewhat distorted, upon calm reflection, it is undeniable. A relative of mine once passionately loved a dancer, and they mutually promised to marry. He forced his parents to break off his engagement with his fiancée in the countryside and cohabited with the dancer. However, after cohabitation, the dancer, being accustomed to extravagance, could not restrain her spending, causing him severe financial strain. At the same time, the dancer, accustomed to the life of red lights and green wine, was not used to settling down as a young mistress. Due to occasional arguments, the couple clashed. Then, the dancer initiated a lawsuit for divorce. After this experience, my relative suddenly awoke and re-engaged a matchmaker to propose to the former fiancée's family and remarry. This happened four years ago, and they have two children. His wife still treats him with the same sincerity and respect as at the beginning of their marriage, and both are very satisfied.

I think plain boiled water may indeed be more meaningful than tea and coffee.

The Transposed Phoenixes

— Written by Zhang Henshui

Chapter 3: Fine Rain and Slanting Wind Still Leave Traces; Quiet Night, Alone Writing a Letter of Severance

As he sat down to calm himself, he couldn't help but reach into his pocket and pull out the letter. He divided the three sheets of paper into two parts. First, he folded two sheets and put them back in the envelope, leaving one sheet to hold in his hands and read. He put the other envelope in the desk drawer, blocking the drawer's opening as if someone were about to open it and snatch the letter. He read all three sheets of paper one by one, and finally, he tapped the table lightly, made up his mind again, quickly put the letter away, and then leaned over the table to write a letter. But after writing only one side, he suddenly remembered something else, immediately stood up, covered the written sheet with a stack of blank paper, then pulled out two of his favorite magazines from the bookshelf, placed them on the table, and casually flipped through them, finding a novel written by Zhang Litian and reading it twice. One of the translated novels had the following dialogue:

Lina, tell me honestly, don't you love me? I love you, and you love me. Besides this, what other requirements are there for the union of a man and a woman? What I mean by union is not necessarily marriage, but simply that in this world, we two are the most in love, and each gains a kind of spiritual comfort. At least one can believe that in the universe, besides oneself, there are others who are not completely irrelevant. As for formal union, it is difficult to satisfy everyone's wishes, but it doesn't matter if it doesn't. What I seek is someone in the universe whom I respect and love, and to whom I can entrust my life's faith. If you don't love me, I will think the same. If you love me, then my love for you will be even stronger. But you keep your love for me hidden in your heart, not letting me know. I truly cannot understand why. If you say that you know I love you, and it might be detrimental to me, then you can endure it. That is still understandable. But you know it, and I already know that you love me. If you could just say one word of love, I would transform into a heavenly horse, born to fly into the sky…"

After reading it, Menglan closed the book, propped her head with both hands, and stared blankly at the lamp. She opened the book again and read it again. She couldn't help but nod twice. The solitary lamp standing quietly at that moment also grew brighter, because it illuminated the person sitting opposite it, and many smiles had appeared on her face. She put the magazines back on the bookshelf. She pulled out the sheet of paper she had written and tore it to pieces. All of it was thrown into the spittoon. She said to herself, "Just ignore it. Why reply to the letter?" So she extracted Guoshi's letter for the third time, and read it for the third time. After half an hour, she could almost recite the words in the letter. She snorted to herself, spread out the paper for the third time, and began to write again. This time it wasn't as difficult as writing the previous sheet. The familiar words in the letter, as well as the dialogue in that novel, evoked many contrasting thoughts. Without pausing, she wrote three sheets of paper in one breath. (45)

Hot Chitchat

— Rongyu

"A calm heart brings natural coolness" is a comforting lie. People working under the scorching sun, no matter how calm their hearts are, won't stop complaining about the heat. Conversely, people sitting in air-conditioned rooms, chewing on colorful ice cream, won't break a sweat no matter how wildly they think.

The song sung by the White Day Rat in the Water Margin's "Capturing the Birthday Presents Intelligently" is truly filled with tears of heat and a sense of injustice. I wonder how many people who read it can appreciate its meaning. The poem says: "The red sun scorches like fire, the rice in the fields is half withered. The farmer's heart is like boiling soup; the sons of nobles wave their fans." Luckily, this poem was written by someone from a previous generation. If it were written by a modern person, it would definitely have a "proletarian" writer's title added to it.

In the "Notes from the Thatched Cottage of Close Observations," it says: "A scholar lived in a small, cramped room facing west. During the hot summer afternoons, the sun would shine so intensely that he would become mentally disturbed and wished he could burn the house down. One day, he took a nap in the room and dreamed that he was captured by the King of Hell and subjected to the torture of knife mountains and boiling cauldrons, suffering unbearably. He also dreamed of sailing on the sea, where the waves were turbulent. Soon, the waves capsized the boat, and he was drowning. He woke up in great fear and realized that he had not been tortured or shipwrecked. Feeling at ease, he felt cool all over. At this moment, he looked at the narrow room and the cramped bed and thought they were more comfortable than jade palaces!" This passage carries some philosophy. "A hungry person readily takes food, a thirsty person readily takes drink" – this is the same principle, and heat is no exception.

Cold news: "Ice Cream Manufacturing Methods" is the work of expert experience. The contents detail the manufacturing process of various colors and flavors of ice cream, as well as its relationship with human health. The writing is concise and clear. The entire book has eight chapters, about seventy pages in length. The manufacturing method is simple and easy, possible for everyone. The price is two dimes per copy. Readers can write to Shanghai Post Office Box 1737. We were honored to receive two copies yesterday and are introducing it here.

Water and Milk Blend?

—

Record of What Was Seen

— (Wu Jiren)

Leaning over the goldfish bowl, I watched the many young fish of this year, seeing them grow day by day. From their tiny, needle-like bodies, one could see the red marks of the bloodworms they had eaten in their bellies. The abdomen of the small fish, in fact the entire body, was gradually developing. As the saying goes, "Growing longer by the day and bigger by the night," I also say this about goldfish.

However, while the small fish themselves are growing, a kind of harmful insect, the "gill worm," also eats the small fish and grows even faster. At first, when setting up the bowl, weren't water plants added? Those tiny "gill worms" invisible to the naked eye had already been brought into the bowl with the water plants. Every day, I saw many small fish floating on the surface of the bowl with their tails dead, some with their heads and bodies separated, and some with their heads and tails missing. This was entirely due to the gill worms.

Grown gill worms are over an inch long, completely like "shrimp," except they have no antennae on their heads, and their heads are flat. A pair of pincers is near their mouths. The small fish have no chance once they are caught by them. Therefore, the gill worms in the fish bowl must be caught quickly, otherwise, the entire bowl of fish will be killed by them.

Also, the growth of several thousand small fish will not be uniform. After a month and a half, some are already very large, while others are still very tiny. At this time, as soon as the water fleas in the bowl are eaten, the large fish will eat the small fish. Such tragic scenes of infighting will occur frequently. If discovered, the large ones must immediately be caught and raised separately.

In-fighting, the weak being the prey of the strong, this is the law of natural selection. Goldfish still have humans to kill the harmful insects. What about humans, the most intelligent of all creatures? They are pitiful enough.

Feature Article

Early Summer in the Inner Garden

— Huo Xueming

"Excuse me, please stop for a moment!" It was still the man dragging the old poet, raising his hand and shouting.

"Why stop for a moment?" The person with the purplish-red face, pushing the copper basin hat on his forehead, said.

"We want to take pictures." The man raising his hand sounded like he was begging for forgiveness.

"Take pictures of your mother! What's it got to do with the old man? This isn't your home!" The person with the purplish-red face rolled his eyes and pushed the man aside, heading straight into the gap in the circle. He sneered, "What a joke! You're allowed to take pictures! We're not allowed to walk! Do you understand? This is everyone's garden..."

A huge round of applause erupted from all directions. The lines of people who had been squinting and making a circle to watch the excitement were broken up by these words and gradually became chaotic. The man and woman who were taking pictures also mingled in the commotion and bitterly drilled through the hole. I immediately turned to look at the old poet, wanting to subtly seek his opinion on this matter with a look of doubt. The old poet smiled at me and said:

"Isn't this a pretty good photo? Let's go. It's going to rain!"

I raised my eyes to the low sky and saw that the gray, decadent clouds had already dissipated, revealing a single scale of sunlight leaking from the gaps in the leaves. I had to foolishly ask:

"It won't rain; the weather is turning for the better!"

"Oh! Who knows? Do you dare to decide that there won't be piercing pain following extreme joy?"

That iron-like quiet word proved its value half a cigarette later. What reason could I still use to justify it? I could only slowly help him go home. The evening sun was excellent, but in the warm breeze, I don't know from where, thin threads of rain were sent--this was the sign of early summer. (The End)

—"Gonorrhea"—

Secret Treatment for Nocturnal Emission

— Physician Liu Zhimin

The number of young men and women suffering from nocturnal emission is truly countless.
