Dog Hairdressing Company

— Yun Hai

The Shanghai Bund is truly full of wonders. Not to mention anything else, just taking "dogs" as an example, there are so many variations. The dog racing track uses dogs as a joke, providing gambling entertainment for gentlemen, and dog doctors specialize in treating foreign dogs for various difficult and complicated ailments like colds and coughs, which have now become commonplace. Not long ago, there was also a new trend, which was the dog restaurant, specially opened for our Chinese and foreign dog-owning class of dog gentlemen and ladies, to "patronize our store," with attentive service, doing whatever they want. In the past, it was rare to see dogs sitting in cars, enjoying the breeze with electric fans; now it is not so foolish, even if you see dog gentlemen and dog ladies eating in dog restaurants that are better than people's restaurants, you will not be surprised by that solemn gentlemanly posture. This is also a sign of urban prosperity.

Now some people are worried about the "hairdressing" problems of dog gentlemen and dog ladies. According to a special report from a certain newspaper, dog hairdressing companies (Cut Dogs Hamr Co.) have been found successively on Yidingpan Road and Lafayette Road, specializing in cutting and shaving dog hair for the dog-owning class. These companies are like barber shops, with various styles and prices ranging from one and a half yuan, two yuan, four yuan, with five yuan being the highest. Cutting takes twenty minutes. The dog feels no pain during cutting. It is said that since these dog hairdressing companies opened, many dog owners have gone to do business, and the business seems to be very good.

Gentlemen seem to have a special fondness for "livestock." A long time ago, we heard about the organization of "animal protection associations," and they issued orders to restrict and even prohibit the ugly abuse of "livestock." However, we have never heard anyone say that they want to organize "poor people protection associations" or "unemployed protection associations." This shows that gentlemen's "livestock" are also "uniquely blessed and without fault." According to this logic, it is not unreasonable for dog hairdressing companies to give preferential treatment to "dogs." Although some poor people cannot get their hair cut even once a year, the "livestock" of noble gentlemen get a haircut, and the minimum price is half a foreign dollar. Looking at it this way, it seems to be too generous to dogs and too stingy to "poor people." However, as long as we fundamentally understand that this social system is not generous to "poor people," but on the contrary exploits them, then we can be "relieved."

Visit to the Baoan Nursing Home

— Fang Zhou

(Special Report from this Newspaper) The second branch of the Baoan Nursing Home in Jiangyuan Lane in this city officially opened on July 1st; I once drove to the home to visit. Later, I wanted to know more about the history and organization of the home, so yesterday afternoon, I made a special trip to the first home on Baoan Road in the South City for a visit.

The Baoan Nursing Home is an affiliated charitable organization of the Shanghai Charity Association. It was founded in the 19th year of the Republic of China, which is about six or seven years ago. It is said that the head of the Shanghai Charity Association is a Mr. Qi from Suzhou, who runs many charitable undertakings. Currently, in addition to this Baoan Nursing Home, the Shanghai Charity Association also includes Tongren Fuyuan Hall, Tongren Fuyuan Branch Hall, Vagrant Work Training Center, Infant Nursery, Lishai Small Vegetable Market, Puyi Vocational Training Center, Women and Children Relief Institute, and no less than a dozen other places; in addition, there is also a poverty relief institute in Suzhou, which currently houses four or five hundred people.

Here, I would like to introduce what I learned from my impressions to the public:

Admission Procedures The home, based on the fact that homeless elderly people often wander the streets, and because of their old age, they cannot support themselves and have nowhere to turn, which is a very miserable situation. Therefore, they aim to take in lonely elderly people over the age of sixty who are truly helpless—only men are accepted, not women. The first step in the admission process is to register at the home, and after approval, you must find a suitable guarantor. After the home sends staff to investigate and verify the facts, you can formally enter the home. However, those with family members and those under the age of sixty are refused admission. No fees are required upon admission, and all living necessities and clothing bedding are provided by the home.

Management Situation The management methods of the home are very complete: for example, the elderly people in the home are all assigned numbers, and other utensils, towels, clothes, and seats are also numbered, and everyone must not occupy each other, so as to avoid disputes.

There are one hundred and eighty wardrobes in the storage room, all with numbers on them, and each person can use one. There are also staff in the room to manage. In the bedroom, there are ten single iron beds arranged in each room. In winter, there is a mattress and a quilt, and now there is a mat and a thin quilt, also with numbers. Furthermore, among the ten people in each room, two capable people are appointed as the head and deputy head of the room. A sign is nailed to the door of the room, and the names of each person and the head and deputy head are written on it. All notices in the home must be conveyed by the head and deputy head, and if anything happens in the room, or if the elderly have any needs, the head and deputy head will contact the office. The dining tables in the dining hall are arranged very neatly, like desks in a classroom. Each table seats nine people, and the seats are also numbered. Each person must sit according to the number, and each number

Page 20

has a small drawer in which each person's bowls and chopsticks are placed, and everyone has an enamel cup for drinking tea. In a corridor, there are also many individual bamboo chairs, one for each person, which they can move around at any time; they can freely sit wherever they like.

The elderly people in the home are absolutely not allowed to go out at ordinary times, and if they violate the rules of the home, they will be educated or slightly reprimanded, and those who continue to be wicked will be expelled, but this situation rarely happens.

Daily Life Their daily life is very mechanized. Three meals a day: porridge in the morning, rice at noon, and half porridge and half rice in the evening. They eat vegetarian food all year round. Usually, there is one dish per person, and there are four days of extra dishes per month, which are the 2nd, 8th, 16th, and 24th of each month. On these four days, each person has two bowls of side dishes per meal. They get a haircut every half month, and now they must take a bath once a day.

After eating, they can all freely find entertainment in the home, each according to their own preferences, or chant Buddhist scriptures, or read books and newspapers, or take a walk and chat, or sleep, or plant flowers and water vegetables, and planting flowers and watering vegetables can also get rewards from the home. If they are happy to make something useful, then the home will also provide them with the things they need; but they are absolutely prohibited from making noise and arguing.

About Expenses The home was originally established by the Shanghai Charity Association, so all expenses are allocated by the Shanghai Charity Association. Currently, the home consumes more than one stone of rice per day on average (slightly less in summer). Including other clothing, utensils, vegetables, oil, salt, and the salaries of staff and workers, it costs more than 10,000 yuan per year. The land and houses are all owned by the Shanghai Charity Association.

Treatment of Illness and Death The home is also responsible for the elderly people who fall ill. Those who are seriously ill are sent to the hospital, and those who are mildly ill are treated in the home's infirmary with doctors and nurses on duty day and night. If they die, if relatives are willing to come to collect the body, they are allowed to do so. If no one comes to collect the body, it will be taken care of by the home.

A Glimpse of the Home's Location The home has more than forty acres of land, with a total of seventy-two rooms. Although the houses are single-story, they are very spacious, and each room has two windows at the back. The architectural style is also new, with glass doors and windows. There are two large courtyards and two small courtyards in the front and back, all with corridors around them, and the air is very well ventilated. There is a flower bed in the center of the fire courtyard, planted with various flowers. In the front, there is also a small horticultural field, covering more than twenty acres, in the middle of which, in addition to a small river, there is also a crop room and a small flower room, where many melons, fruits, vegetables, and potted flowers are planted. These are left behind by them in loneliness, or spontaneously, and it is said that the home also rewards those who do these things. That is, they are willing to do it for a day, and there will be a reward for a day. However, these are all based on their own initiative, and the home does not force them.

The equipment in the housing section includes eighteen bedrooms, one storage room, one Buddhist hall, one infirmary, one medicine cooking room, one kitchen, one washing room, one study room, one dining hall, one office, one staff bedroom, one worker bedroom, one staff toilet, one worker toilet, one water heater, one room, one item storage room, and several elderly people's urinals. As for those places, there are three or four rooms combined into one room, and there are also one or two rooms combined into one room, and the light and air in each room are very sufficient, and the environment can be said to be extremely quiet.

The home has now taken in one hundred and eighty elderly people. Because it is full, it is impossible to take in more people for a while. However, there are still many referrals from various institutions and registrations. Therefore, a second home has been set up in Jiangyuan Lane. It was originally a poverty clinic, also run by the Shanghai Charity Association. There are more than ten rooms, and a wide building, and a large courtyard. The air, light, and environment are similar to the first home, but it lacks a piece of open space. The organization and methods are also based on the first home, but the limit is only forty people, so when it opened on July 1, the quota was already full, and it will only be possible to take in more people after the original quota is reduced.

In terms of employees, there are currently seven staff members and more than ten workers in the first home, and four staff members and six or seven workers in the second home.

In recent years, various provinces have promoted respect for the elderly and held respect for the elderly conferences: but what they respect are only some rich elderly people, and those poor elderly people in the vast stratum who are forgotten by people are not given attention.

Save these poor elderly people!

Smuggling Comes Amidst Rampant Voices: Let's Talk About Women's Decorations

— Wen Hai

China is a semi-colonial country and a battleground for the sale of surplus goods by various powers. Therefore, various powers can use their superior position in China to systematically extract and exploit the Chinese people in all aspects!

The smuggling problem in North China is now becoming increasingly serious. It is precisely the implementation of a consistent and vicious policy of planned aggression against China. The increasing expansion of the smuggling problem will not only affect the Chinese government's fiscal revenue, but also accelerate the destruction of Chinese industry and commerce. They want to make China's weak national industry forever in a state of decline and depression.

It is said that among the smuggled goods, in addition to piece goods, food, rayon, and children's toys, most of them are women's cosmetics, which account for an important position. How much of China's annual deficit is spent on women's perfumes, powders, rouge, hair gel, etc.? The customs report has already been published in various newspapers, so I will not repeat it here.

The love of beauty is human nature, especially women's fondness for beauty. They believe that decoration is produced under the condition of love of beauty, especially for women in prosperous cities. Everyone competes to be beautiful and unique, and the entire life time is almost entirely occupied by decoration. On the bodies of these beauty lovers, the waste of time and the loss of money for the women in the country are probably difficult to count.

A news item was published in the Shen Bao's June 17th local news column, which talked about the fashionable clothes of 1936, which detailed that Westerners wear summer cloth made in China. Summer cloth is woven from linen, which is durable, beautiful, and cheap. Westerners actually regard summer cloth as the most fashionable clothes this year. Looking back at the country, they pick up summer cloth and wear imported silk gauze, foreign money. It is not worth it.

If the smuggling problem is not resolved, it will lead our country to death. This is so dangerous! However, how can the smuggling problem be thoroughly resolved? It is useless for the government to promulgate anti-smuggling regulations and severely punish smugglers. To solve the problem at the root, I hope that the people of the country will cooperate to resist the smuggling incident.

The oppression of imperialism has reached the final stage. I hope that women across the country will quickly wake up and take on this arduous responsibility to save the Chinese nation from danger. Like the women of Abyssinia, go to the front line with their husbands! Arise! People who don't want to be slaves!

Wheat

— Chen Liang

Early in the morning, Uncle Genshou stood at the foot of the ladder, his hands on his hips, looking up at the dimly lit attic and nagging: "Are you suffering from lazy jaundice? You look like you're going to die. Do you know that the grain market closes early in hot weather? Hurry up, hurry up, you lazy thing..."

A woman's head appeared in the dimly lit attic, tied with a calico headscarf. Her face was sad. She slowly fastened the basket with rope buckles. The basket was full of wheat. She was not sick, but the glossy shape of each grain of wheat, the bright earthy yellow color, and the aroma that stimulated appetite aroused endless sadness in her heart. From bearing the scorching sun, crouching in the sharp awns, letting the humid and hot ground vapor scorch her eyes until they were blurred, and grabbing the sickle to cut the field...until throwing out the grains, drying them again and again, moving them to the attic, throwing them into the wooden cabinet, it hasn't even been a month, but now they have to be sold.

"Is this basket enough?" she said, while slowly lowering the basket of wheat. Her attachment to the money also dropped to the ground. Aunt Genshou was not a very stingy woman, but she was really reluctant to sell the wheat.

"One basket, two baskets, it's not like I'm selling them to eat, gamble, or whore. Whose field did you plant? Don't you have to pay rent? How much soybean cake did you put down? Don't you have to pay back the money? Don't you have to pay the high interest on the ten coppers from Dalong? You sit at home, what do you know? The wheat market is good these days. If you don't take advantage of the situation to sell some and pay people back, can you delay it? Do you think I want to owe people with a straight face...?" Uncle Genshou lowered his head, untied the rope buckle at the edge of the basket, and kept nagging as he measured it with a斗(dǒu). When he used his palm to scrape the wheat on the surface of the 斗(dǒu), he felt a smooth touch and couldn't help but feel sad in his heart. This sadness was hidden in his nagging words.

Genshou always said in front of people—even if he met a stranger passing by at the crossroads:

"Alas, who doesn't think I'm a hardworking and ingratiating person? I don't waste a penny all year round. I don't touch a pipe, I don't drink liquor, I don't step into a teahouse, let alone gamble. But I don't know where the harvests go after one harvest after another. As soon as they come from the field, they have to be sold. Later, I have to borrow a升(shēng) here and a 斗(dǒu) there. I myself don't believe it. Year after year, who am I busy for?"

Sometimes, he even sighed like this to his own woman.

When Aunt Genshou lowered the second basket of wheat to the ground, he slipped out a series of repetitive nagging: "You sit at home, what do you know? The wheat market is good these days. If you don't take advantage of the situation to sell some..." complaining about his woman's words. Aunt Genshou couldn't help but wipe the sweat beads that were flowing to the edge of her eyelids in the attic and said, "The market is good, the wheat market is good, but why doesn't the Guilin grandpa's family, who owes hundreds of 担(dàn) of wheat, sell it even when the market owner comes to the door? Doesn't he know the market is good?" It seemed that she held a powerful citation to refute him.

However, this citation became a kind of stimulation in Uncle Genshou's ears, and the reaction to the stimulation was another round of nagging: "You said Guilin grandpa's family owes hundreds of 担(dàn) of wheat, do you know why he doesn't sell it? You won't know even if you die. He doesn't need money, only people owe him, not him owing people. He hoards it at home to prepare to kill the poor in the future. His brother-in-law runs a flour mill, and he is very well-informed about the market. What is he worried about! He will wait until everyone is holding their stomachs before opening the warehouse to bargain. Can we compare with him? You are daydreaming, you are having a fever..."

Aunt Genshou hoisted the empty basket up to the attic, and her sad face disappeared into the darkness.

Opening "Lament of the Fifth Watch"

The Jingde Banquet Tower strikes the first drum. The imperial concubine sits alone, tears streaming down her face. Only because her husband is away with no news. His whereabouts are uncertain. Could it be that he has fallen in love with another woman in another country, more talented than I am? Therefore, the news is silent and difficult to grasp. Making me sit and listen to the second drum, my breath is difficult to extinguish. My love, I think of the flowery words you said before you left. Saying that once you arrive in the capital, you will wave your brush. Good news will convey beauty. But alas, I am waiting for letters but none arrive. It is like a kite with a broken string, its voice and breath gone. The third watch passes. The fourth watch passes. I am alone and desolate. My tormentor, alas, my heart is tied in knots, my hatred is difficult to extinguish. The imperial concubine sighs and seldom consults. That miserable situation is even more difficult to describe. Alas... My lord. If you cannot let go of a loving, righteous, and beautiful sheep. You can also bring her back to share the nest. Two horses can be in the same trough. I will never be jealous. Sisters will call each other happily. I only hate that my lord's heart is not as kind as mine. Leaving good intentions to hide in a crowd of people. What is bitter is that the long night and short dream are difficult to pass. I only hear the sound of the fifth drum faintly knocking from the city tower. One sound low. One sound high. One sound far. One sound floating. Sound echoes and laments. Passing so desolately. The imperial concubine feels even more bored. Suddenly, I hear the sound of insects chirping like weeping on all sides. Lamenting the fifth watch ruined the beauty. Even your heart of iron will be moved.

Extra Sounds

Gu Hong died, Jin Peiyu seems very lonely.

Little Changzhou has returned from Nanjing after serving as an official, and is recently engaged to a certain young lady, which seems very good.

The Lingling Singing Society Drama Troupe is preparing to perform "Struggling After Being Afraid", directed by Zhou Tingmao. It is said that the work has been very intense recently.

Yuexing Singing # Society welcomes male and female comrades who love singing to join. Please send a letter to No. 8 Bailinan Branch Road, the society.

Since its publication, the Fengming Advertising Agency's Fengming Monthly has been well received by listeners. From the fourth issue, it will add nationwide. It is heard that the company originally set the price at 5 jiao for the whole year. The current preferential period for ordering the fourth issue is only 2 jiao for postage. There are 12 issues throughout the year, published on the 5th of each month. Subscribers from this and other places should enclose sufficient postage of 2 jiao and send a letter directly to the company on the fifth floor of Shanghai Great World, and it will be sent immediately.

The Shanghai Huanqiu Harmonica Association was founded by Mr. Bao Mingshan. It has been established for more than a year. Because the teaching is serious, the results are quite remarkable. Recently, it has been heard that Mr. Bao, at the request of harmonica enthusiasts in this city, has specially added a harmonica special class, which is scheduled to officially open on December 12th (Sunday) at 7:30 PM. Membership fees and tuition fees are all waived. Those who are interested in studying this music can go to No. 11 Yuancheng Li, Lane 157, Anren Street, Xinbeimen, in the city to register and join.

Shanghai Caishi Road, Lane 16, No. 7 Yuanchang Radio Station has recently released a variety of scripts written by Li Chang, including "Northeast Blood", "Resurrection", "Love Rival", "Husband Loves Wife", "Respect Each Other Like Guests", and "Reforming Couples", a total of six types. All walks of life are welcome to send letters to request them. Each type includes 5 cents for postage. The whole set only costs 3 jiao for the cost. Mr. Li will personally broadcast various scripts on the station every night from 1:30 AM.

Movies

Elastic Girl Published Today

The Yingwu News Agency publishes the "Elastic Girl" weekly, which is a publication specializing in news about dance halls and dancers. The content is rich and interesting. The inaugural issue has been published today and sells for 5 French currency per copy. It is sold at all newspaper stalls. The contents of the inaugural issue include anecdotes about Liang sisters, Chen Jingfang, Sun Lifang, Zhao Lianfang, Zhao Manli, Niu Lulu, Little Sister Li, Little Sister Chen, Wang Mary... and other popular dance stars.

New Nine O'Clock Dance Troupe

Performing at the Carlton Theatre

Two years ago, there was a famous American dance troupe called the "Nine O'Clock Dance Troupe" that performed in Shanghai. At that time, it was praised by the people of Shanghai and its business was excellent. Today, the "New Nine O'Clock Dance Troupe" performing at the Carlton is based on the "Nine O'Clock Dance Troupe", plus a lot of talented people and new tricks, which is a hundred times more exciting than the previous performance. The content includes enchanting exotic dances, soul-stirring love songs, intoxicating music, and hilarious comedies. Everything is a modern aesthetic. It is said that it is as tempting as the most famous midnight dance troupe in Paris. The theater does not increase seat prices in order to popularize it.

Marriage Statistics of Hollywood Actors

— Mars

Average of only six years of history per couple

From the union of 200 Hollywood actors, each couple can only maintain an average of five years, eleven months, and seven days of history. The longest is seven years and six months, and the shortest is four years and six months.

Last year, thirty female stars went through divorces, and this year they got married again! (According to American law, couples who have divorced must wait a period of time before they can marry again.)

Of course, there are exceptions for some stars who have been married for a long time. Such as Mr. and Mrs. George Ali for thirty-five years, Mr. and Mrs. Harashoto for twenty-two years, Mr. and Mrs. Eddie Condon for twenty-one years, Mr. and Mrs. Warner Baxter for twenty years, Mr. and Mrs. Paul Muni for fourteen years, Mr. and Mrs. Locke for twelve years, Lyon Barrymore for twelve years, and Mr. and Mrs. Jimmy Gleason for twenty-eight years.

The stars who divorced last year and can marry this year by the court include Halo, Kinekna, Anna Panqi, Manlai Astor, Dorothy Costello, Berrymore, Elisa Lundy, Nancy Carroll, Virginia Kelly, Ames, Blondell, and Zanakna, and more than ten others.
